<h2>코퍼스 — 005_subagents-collab/05_ai_subagent.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Aider — Subagents / Collaboration</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>110_aider/</code> — dual-model <strong>architect → editor</strong> pipeline in <code>architect_coder.py</code>; <strong><code>AskCoder</code></strong> for read-only Q&#x26;A; <strong>no parallel subagent scheduler</strong>, no worker pool, no cross-session agent IDs.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Aider's closest collaboration primitive is <strong>architect mode</strong>: one model (architect) drafts an implementation plan in natural language; after optional human approval, a nested <strong><code>Coder.create()</code></strong> session spins up a second <strong>editor</strong> model that applies concrete edits. <strong><code>AskCoder</code></strong> provides a read-only analysis mode without spawning a second agent. All handoffs are <strong>sequential</strong>, in-process, sharing the same <code>io</code> REPL — not multi-agent orchestration.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  User["User /architect or --architect"] --> AC["ArchitectCoder&#x3C;br/>edit_format=architect"]
  AC --> LLM1["main_model (architect)&#x3C;br/>ArchitectPrompts"]
  LLM1 --> Plan["partial_response_content&#x3C;br/>change plan text"]
  Plan --> Gate{"auto_accept_architect&#x3C;br/>or confirm_ask?"}
  Gate -->|declined| Stop["return — no edits"]
  Gate -->|approved| Create["Coder.create(from_coder=self)&#x3C;br/>main_model=editor_model"]
  Create --> EC["Editor coder&#x3C;br/>editor-diff / etc."]
  EC --> Run["editor_coder.run(with_message=plan)"]
  Run --> Merge["move_back_cur_messages()&#x3C;br/>sync cost + commit hashes"]
  Ask["/ask → AskCoder"] --> LLM2["main_model&#x3C;br/>AskPrompts — no edits"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Coder class registry (<code>coders/__init__.py</code>)</h2>
<p>All edit formats are plain Python subclasses registered by <code>edit_format</code> string:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/aider/coders/__init__.py:18-34
__all__ = [
    HelpCoder, AskCoder, Coder, EditBlockCoder, ...
    ArchitectCoder,
    EditorEditBlockCoder, EditorWholeFileCoder, EditorDiffFencedCoder,
    ContextCoder,
]
</code></pre>
<p><code>Coder.create()</code> (<code>base_coder.py:190-194</code>) iterates <code>__all__</code>, matches <code>coder.edit_format == edit_format</code>, instantiates. No plugin loader, no TOML agent definitions — <strong>format string IS the role selector</strong>.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Class</th>
<th><code>edit_format</code></th>
<th>Role</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>AskCoder</code></td>
<td><code>ask</code></td>
<td>Read-only Q&#x26;A</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>ArchitectCoder</code></td>
<td><code>architect</code></td>
<td>Plan-only; spawns editor</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>EditBlockCoder</code></td>
<td><code>diff</code></td>
<td>Standard edits</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>EditorEditBlockCoder</code></td>
<td><code>editor-diff</code></td>
<td>Editor pass for architect</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>ContextCoder</code></td>
<td><code>context</code></td>
<td>Surrounding code context view</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<h2>2. <code>Coder.create()</code> — nested session factory (<code>base_coder.py:125-201</code>)</h2>
<h3>2.1 Resolution order</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/aider/coders/base_coder.py:125-148
@classmethod
def create(self, main_model=None, edit_format=None, io=None, from_coder=None, ...):
    if not main_model:
        main_model = from_coder.main_model if from_coder else models.Model(...)
    if edit_format is None:
        edit_format = from_coder.edit_format if from_coder else main_model.edit_format
    if not io and from_coder:
        io = from_coder.io
</code></pre>
<h3>2.2 Context carry-over from <code>from_coder</code> (<code>:153-187</code>)</h3>
<p>When switching or nesting coders:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Copied field</th>
<th>Purpose</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>fnames</code>, <code>read_only_fnames</code></td>
<td>Same file context</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>done_messages</code>, <code>cur_messages</code></td>
<td>Chat continuity</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>aider_commit_hashes</code></td>
<td>Undo scope</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>commands</code> (cloned)</td>
<td>Slash commands</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>total_cost</code>, token counters</td>
<td>Billing aggregate</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>file_watcher</code></td>
<td>File change detection</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>If <code>edit_format</code> changes and history exists, <strong><code>summarize_all()</code></strong> may compress <code>done_messages</code> to avoid confusing the new LLM with old edit-format examples (<code>:161-168</code>).</p>
<p><strong>Architect editor pass</strong> sets <code>summarize_from_coder=False</code> explicitly (<code>architect_coder.py:32</code>) so architect plan stays in <code>cur_messages</code> for the editor's <code>with_message</code> injection.</p>
<h3>2.3 Unknown format</h3>
<p>Raises <code>UnknownEditFormat</code> with list of valid formats (<code>:196-201</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. <code>AskCoder</code> — read-only sub-mode (<code>ask_coder.py</code>, <code>ask_prompts.py</code>)</h2>
<h3>3.1 Class definition</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/aider/coders/ask_coder.py:5-9
class AskCoder(Coder):
    """Ask questions about code without making any changes."""
    edit_format = "ask"
    gpt_prompts = AskPrompts()
</code></pre>
<p>Inherits full <code>Coder</code> loop but prompts forbid substantive edits:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/aider/coders/ask_prompts.py:7-18
main_system = """Act as an expert code analyst.
Answer questions about the supplied code.
...
"""
overeager_prompt = """Do not return fully detailed code or full diffs.
Describe the needed changes or give a plan.
"""
</code></pre>
<p><strong>No <code>reply_completed</code> override</strong> — AskCoder never spawns a nested editor. Single-model, single-pass.</p>
<h3>3.2 Entry points</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Entry</th>
<th>Path</th>
<th>Behavior</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>/ask [prompt]</code></td>
<td><code>commands.py:1182-1184</code></td>
<td><code>_generic_chat_command(args, "ask")</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/ask</code> alone</td>
<td><code>commands.py:1207-1209</code></td>
<td><code>cmd_chat_mode("ask")</code> — persistent mode switch</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>--chat-mode ask</code></td>
<td><code>args.py:165-169</code></td>
<td>Startup format</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>3.3 <code>_generic_chat_command</code> flow (<code>commands.py:1206-1230</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">coder = Coder.create(
    io=self.io,
    from_coder=self.coder,
    edit_format=edit_format,
    summarize_from_coder=False,
)
coder.run(user_msg)
raise SwitchCoder(from_coder=coder, ...)  # restore prior mode after one-shot
</code></pre>
<p>One-shot <code>/ask question</code> runs AskCoder for a single turn, then raises <code>SwitchCoder</code> to revert to previous edit format without summarizing — keeping architect/code mode context intact.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. <code>ArchitectCoder</code> — full dual-model flow (<code>architect_coder.py</code>)</h2>
<h3>4.1 Class hierarchy</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/aider/coders/architect_coder.py:6-9
class ArchitectCoder(AskCoder):
    edit_format = "architect"
    gpt_prompts = ArchitectPrompts()
    auto_accept_architect = False  # class default; overridden by __init__ kwarg
</code></pre>
<p>Extends <strong>AskCoder</strong> (read-only planning DNA) but overrides <code>reply_completed</code> to trigger editor pass.</p>
<h3>4.2 Architect system prompt (<code>architect_prompts.py:7-17</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">main_system = """Act as an expert architect engineer and provide direction to your editor engineer.
Study the change request and the current code.
Describe how to modify the code to complete the request.
The editor engineer will rely solely on your instructions, so make them unambiguous and complete.
...
DO NOT show the entire updated function/file/etc!
"""
</code></pre>
<p>Architect output is <strong>instructions</strong>, not fenced edit blocks — editor model interprets plan text.</p>
<h3>4.3 <code>reply_completed()</code> — complete handoff (<code>architect_coder.py:11-48</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">def reply_completed(self):
    content = self.partial_response_content
    if not content or not content.strip():
        return

    if not self.auto_accept_architect and not self.io.confirm_ask("Edit the files?"):
        return

    editor_model = self.main_model.editor_model or self.main_model

    kwargs["main_model"] = editor_model
    kwargs["edit_format"] = self.main_model.editor_edit_format
    kwargs["suggest_shell_commands"] = False
    kwargs["map_tokens"] = 0
    kwargs["total_cost"] = self.total_cost
    kwargs["cache_prompts"] = False
    kwargs["num_cache_warming_pings"] = 0
    kwargs["summarize_from_coder"] = False

    new_kwargs = dict(io=self.io, from_coder=self)
    new_kwargs.update(kwargs)

    editor_coder = Coder.create(**new_kwargs)
    editor_coder.cur_messages = []
    editor_coder.done_messages = []

    editor_coder.run(with_message=content, preproc=False)

    self.move_back_cur_messages("I made those changes to the files.")
    self.total_cost = editor_coder.total_cost
    self.aider_commit_hashes = editor_coder.aider_commit_hashes
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Step-by-step semantics:</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Step</th>
<th>Lines</th>
<th>Meaning</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Empty plan guard</td>
<td><code>:14-15</code></td>
<td>No editor spawn if architect silent</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Human gate</td>
<td><code>:17-18</code></td>
<td><code>confirm_ask("Edit the files?")</code> unless auto-accept</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Editor model pick</td>
<td><code>:22-23</code></td>
<td><code>main_model.editor_model</code> or fallback to architect model</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Editor format</td>
<td><code>:26</code></td>
<td>From <code>main_model.editor_edit_format</code> (e.g. <code>editor-diff</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Disable shell</td>
<td><code>:27</code></td>
<td>Editor should not suggest shell during apply</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Disable repo map</td>
<td><code>:28</code></td>
<td><code>map_tokens=0</code> — editor has full file bodies in chat</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Disable cache warming</td>
<td><code>:30-31</code></td>
<td>Nested pass skips prompt cache pings</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fresh message lists</td>
<td><code>:38-39</code></td>
<td>Editor starts clean cur/done; plan via <code>with_message</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>preproc=False</code></td>
<td><code>:44</code></td>
<td>Skip re-processing plan as user slash commands</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Merge back</td>
<td><code>:46-48</code></td>
<td>Append synthetic user/assistant pair; sync cost/commits</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>4.4 <code>move_back_cur_messages()</code> (<code>base_coder.py:1036-1046</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">def move_back_cur_messages(self, message):
    self.done_messages += self.cur_messages
    self.summarize_start()
    if message:
        self.done_messages += [
            dict(role="user", content=message),
            dict(role="assistant", content="Ok."),
        ]
    self.cur_messages = []
</code></pre>
<p>Architect session folds editor turn into durable history with acknowledgment stub — same pattern as repo map injection.</p>
<h3>4.5 Announcements (<code>base_coder.py:239-244</code>)</h3>
<p>When <code>edit_format == "architect"</code>, startup banner shows both models:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">output = (
    f"Editor model: {main_model.editor_model.name} with"
    f" {main_model.editor_edit_format} edit format"
)
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>5. Editor model configuration (<code>models.py</code>)</h2>
<h3>5.1 Model metadata fields</h3>
<ul>
<li><code>editor_model_name</code>, <code>editor_edit_format</code> on <code>ModelInfo</code> (<code>models.py:145-146</code>).</li>
<li><code>get_editor_model()</code> (<code>:625-645</code>): resolves separate <code>Model</code> instance; prefixes <code>editor-</code> onto diff/whole formats when unset.</li>
</ul>
<h3>5.2 Bundled defaults (<code>resources/model-settings.yml</code>)</h3>
<p>Many models ship with architect pairing, e.g.:</p>
<pre><code class="language-yaml"># Pattern seen throughout model-settings.yml
edit_format: architect
editor_model_name: gpt-4o
editor_edit_format: editor-diff
</code></pre>
<p>CLI overrides: <code>--editor-model</code>, <code>--editor-edit-format</code> (<code>args.py:194+</code>).</p>
<h3>5.3 Sanity check (<code>models.py:1155-1159</code>)</h3>
<p>On startup, if <code>editor_model</code> differs from main and weak models, validates editor model connectivity.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. CLI and slash-command entry</h2>
<h3>6.1 Flags (<code>args.py:171-183</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Flag</th>
<th>Effect</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>--architect</code></td>
<td>Sets <code>edit_format=architect</code> (store_const)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>--auto-accept-architect</code></td>
<td>BooleanOptionalAction, <strong>default True</strong> at argparse level</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>--editor-model</code></td>
<td>Override editor LLM</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>--chat-mode</code></td>
<td>Includes <code>architect</code>, <code>ask</code> in choices</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Note:</strong> <code>ArchitectCoder.auto_accept_architect = False</code> at class level, but <code>base_coder.__init__</code> receives <code>auto_accept_architect=args.auto_accept_architect</code> from main (<code>main.py:1005</code>) — instance attribute wins. Effective default for CLI sessions is <strong>auto-accept True</strong> unless user passes <code>--no-auto-accept-architect</code>.</p>
<h3>6.2 Slash commands (<code>commands.py</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">def cmd_ask(self, args):
    return self._generic_chat_command(args, "ask")

def cmd_architect(self, args):
    return self._generic_chat_command(args, "architect")
</code></pre>
<p>Persistent mode: <code>/architect</code> with no args → <code>cmd_chat_mode("architect")</code>.</p>
<p>Related: <code>/code</code> returns to main edit format (<code>:1186-1188</code>); <code>/ok</code> aliases approval message to code mode (<code>:1198-1204</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. What Aider does NOT implement</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Feature</th>
<th>Codex / multi-agent harnesses</th>
<th>Aider</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Parallel subagents</td>
<td><code>multi_agent_v2</code>, fan-out</td>
<td><strong>Not implemented</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Task tool / spawn</td>
<td><code>task</code> tool + thread manager</td>
<td>Single nested <code>Coder.create()</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Agent IDs / mailboxes</td>
<td>Cross-session messaging</td>
<td>Shared <code>io</code>, one REPL</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Worker pool</td>
<td>Background employees</td>
<td>None</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Subagent specialization</td>
<td>TOML agents, roles</td>
<td><code>edit_format</code> class only</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Autonomous handoff</td>
<td>Model decides to spawn</td>
<td>Architect <strong>always</strong> triggers editor after gate (if plan non-empty)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>External orchestration (jaw employees, custom scripts) required for true multi-agent parallelism.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Comparison: Ask vs Architect vs Code</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Mode</th>
<th>Class</th>
<th>Edits files?</th>
<th>Second model?</th>
<th>Human gate</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>ask</code></td>
<td>AskCoder</td>
<td>No</td>
<td>No</td>
<td>N/A</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>architect</code></td>
<td>ArchitectCoder</td>
<td>Via editor</td>
<td>Yes</td>
<td><code>confirm_ask</code> or auto-accept</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>diff</code> / etc.</td>
<td>EditBlockCoder…</td>
<td>Yes</td>
<td>No</td>
<td>Normal edit flow</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Architect inherits AskCoder's planning-oriented prompts but adds <code>reply_completed</code> editor pipeline. Editor coders (<code>Editor*Coder</code>) are <strong>never</strong> user-selected directly — only via architect handoff or <code>--chat-mode</code> for debugging.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. <code>ContextCoder</code> — related single-agent mode</h2>
<p><code>ContextCoder</code> (<code>context_coder.py:17-18</code>) forces <code>repo_map.refresh = "always"</code> and multiplies map tokens — a <strong>context-expansion</strong> mode, not a subagent. Documented here because <code>/context</code> sits beside <code>/ask</code> and <code>/architect</code> in the mode-switch family (<code>commands.py:1194-1196</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. Parity matrix vs Codex (<code>co</code>)</h2>
<table>

<th>Concern</th>

<hr>
<h2>11. Operational workflow (user perspective)</h2>
<h3>Architect session</h3>
<ol>
<li>User starts <code>aider --architect</code> or <code>/architect refactor the auth module</code></li>
<li>Banner shows architect model + editor model (<code>get_announcements</code>)</li>
<li>Architect model responds with plan text (no auto-applied edits)</li>
<li>Unless <code>--no-auto-accept-architect</code>, user sees <code>Edit the files? [Y/n]</code></li>
<li>On approval, editor model runs with plan as <code>with_message</code>; diffs applied</li>
<li>History records "I made those changes to the files." / "Ok."</li>
<li>User continues in architect mode for next request</li>
</ol>
<h3>Ask session</h3>
<ol>
<li><code>/ask how does RepoMap rank files?</code></li>
<li>AskCoder answers without edit blocks or editor spawn</li>
<li><code>SwitchCoder</code> restores prior mode if one-shot</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<h2>12. Token and context implications</h2>
<ul>
<li>Editor pass sets <strong><code>map_tokens=0</code></strong> — relies on files already in chat, not repo map (<code>architect_coder.py:28</code>).</li>
<li>Editor <strong><code>cur_messages</code> and <code>done_messages</code> cleared</strong> — plan arrives only via <code>run(with_message=content)</code>; prior architect turn messages moved to parent after merge.</li>
<li><strong><code>summarize_from_coder=False</code></strong> on both architect spawn and slash one-shots — avoids losing plan detail to summarizer.</li>
</ul>

1a:["$","$L28","20-axis-05-subagent",{"id":"20-axis-05-subagent","order":22,"tier":"deep","title":"축 05: 서브에이전트","description":"005_subagents-collab/05_ai_subagent.md","lang":"ko","badge":"AXIS","children":["$","div",null,{"dangerouslySetInnerHTML":{"__html":"$3a"}}]}]
3b:T6cfd,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>Aider는 <strong>앱서버가 없는 순수 CLI 도구</strong>다. Codex의 <code>app-server</code> + <code>protocol</code> + <code>client</code> 삼각형과 근본적으로 다르며, Claude Code처럼 단일 프로세스 아키텍처이되, 외형은 더 단순하다. 장기 실행 서버, wire protocol, SDK, IDE 확장이 모두 존재하지 않는다. 유일한 서비스 표면은 대화형 CLI이고, 선택적으로 Streamlit 기반 웹 GUI를 올릴 수 있다.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li>진입점과 부트스트랩</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>1.1 main.py — 부트스트랩 체인</li>
<li>1.2 Coder 클래스 — 핵심 실행 단위</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li>클라이언트 표면</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>2.1 대화형 CLI (기본 모드)</li>
<li>2.2 Streamlit GUI (--gui)</li>
<li>2.3 파이프 모드 (비대화형)</li>
<li>2.4 File Watcher 모드</li>
<li>2.5 ClipboardWatcher</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li>LLM 통합 (LiteLLM)</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>3.1 다중 제공사 지원</li>
<li>3.2 편집 포맷 전략</li>
</ul>
<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD

class InputOutput:
    def __init__(self, pretty, yes_always, ...):
        self.pretty = pretty
        self.yes_always = yes_always

    def get_input(self, ...):
        # prompt_toolkit 기반 사용자 입력
        # 자동완성, 히스토리, 편집 모드 지원

    def confirm_ask(self, question, ...):
        # 사용자 확인 (yes_always이면 자동 승인)

    def tool_output(self, msg, ...):
        # 컬러 코드 적용 출력

<h2>코퍼스 — 006_app-server-client-surfaces/06_ai_surface.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Aider 앱·서버·클라이언트 서피스 분석</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>110_aider/</code> — app/server/client surfaces.</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>⚠️ <strong>오픈소스 분석</strong>: 이 문서는 <code>110_aider/</code> 저장소의 <code>main.py</code>, <code>coders/base_coder.py</code>, <code>commands.py</code>, <code>io.py</code>, <code>gui.py</code> 소스 코드에 기반한다.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Aider는 <strong>앱서버가 없는 순수 CLI 도구</strong>다. Codex의 <code>app-server</code> + <code>protocol</code> + <code>client</code> 삼각형과 근본적으로 다르며, Claude Code처럼 단일 프로세스 아키텍처이되, 외형은 더 단순하다. 장기 실행 서버, wire protocol, SDK, IDE 확장이 모두 존재하지 않는다. 유일한 서비스 표면은 대화형 CLI이고, 선택적으로 Streamlit 기반 웹 GUI를 올릴 수 있다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    subgraph Process["단일 Python 프로세스"]
        Main["main.py\n(args 파서 + 부트스트랩)"]
        Coder["Coder 인스턴스\n(base_coder.py)"]
        Commands["Commands\n(/ 명령어)"]
        IO["InputOutput\n(prompt_toolkit)"]
        LiteLLM["LiteLLM\n(다중 제공사)"]
        Git["GitRepo\n(gitpython)"]
    end

    subgraph Surfaces["클라이언트 표면"]
        CLI["대화형 CLI\n(prompt_toolkit)"]
        GUI["Streamlit GUI\n(gui.py, 선택적)"]
        Pipe["파이프 모드\n(--yes-always)"]
        Watch["File Watcher\n(--watch-files)"]
    end

    Main --> Coder
    Coder --> Commands
    Coder --> IO
    Coder --> LiteLLM
    Coder --> Git
    CLI --> Main
    GUI --> Main
    Pipe --> Main
    Watch --> Main
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. 진입점과 부트스트랩</h2>
<h3>1.1 main.py — 부트스트랩 체인</h3>
<p><code>main()</code> 함수가 전체 부트스트랩을 관리한다. 1,275줄의 단일 함수로, 다음 순서를 따른다 (신뢰도 🟢 높음):</p>
<pre><code>1. Git 저장소 감지 (get_git_root)
2. 설정 파일 탐색 (.aider.conf.yml)
3. ArgumentParser 생성 (get_parser)
4. .env 로드 (load_dotenv_files)
5. 인수 검증 및 환경 변수 설정
6. Analytics 초기화
7. GUI 모드 분기 (--gui)
8. Git 설정 (setup_git)
9. 모델 레지스트리 로딩 (register_models, register_litellm_models)
10. 모델 선택 (select_default_model)
11. Coder 인스턴스 생성
12. 대화 루프 시작
</code></pre>
<h3>1.2 Coder 클래스 — 핵심 실행 단위</h3>
<p><code>Coder</code> 클래스(<code>coders/base_coder.py</code>)가 Aider의 핵심 실행 단위다. 편집 포맷(diff, whole, udiff, architect)에 따라 서브클래스로 분기한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">classDiagram
    class Coder {
        +run(user_message)
        +run_one(user_message)
        +send_message(messages)
        +apply_edits(edits)
        +get_context_from_history()
        +get_repo_map()
    }
    class EditBlockCoder
    class WholeCoder
    class UnifiedDiffCoder
    class ArchitectCoder

    Coder &#x3C;|-- EditBlockCoder
    Coder &#x3C;|-- WholeCoder
    Coder &#x3C;|-- UnifiedDiffCoder
    Coder &#x3C;|-- ArchitectCoder
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>2. 클라이언트 표면</h2>
<h3>2.1 대화형 CLI (기본 모드)</h3>
<p><code>prompt_toolkit</code> 기반 대화형 인터페이스가 기본 표면이다. <code>InputOutput</code> 클래스가 입출력을 추상화한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/io.py — InputOutput 핵심
class InputOutput:
    def __init__(self, pretty, yes_always, ...):
        self.pretty = pretty
        self.yes_always = yes_always

    def get_input(self, ...):
        # prompt_toolkit 기반 사용자 입력
        # 자동완성, 히스토리, 편집 모드 지원

    def confirm_ask(self, question, ...):
        # 사용자 확인 (yes_always이면 자동 승인)

    def tool_output(self, msg, ...):
        # 컬러 코드 적용 출력

    def tool_error(self, msg, ...):
        # 에러 출력 (빨간색)
</code></pre>
<h3>2.2 Streamlit GUI (--gui)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-bash">aider --gui
</code></pre>
<p><code>gui.py</code>가 Streamlit 웹 앱을 올린다. 대화 히스토리, 파일 선택, 모델 선택 등을 웹 UI로 제공한다. 별도 서버 프로세스가 아니라 Streamlit의 내장 서버를 사용한다 (신뢰도 🟢 높음).</p>
<pre><code>launch_gui():
  1. write_streamlit_credentials() — 이메일 프롬프트 비활성화
  2. streamlit.web.cli.main(["run", gui.__file__, ...])
  3. 브라우저 자동 열기
</code></pre>
<h3>2.3 파이프 모드 (비대화형)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-bash">echo "fix the bug in main.py" | aider --yes-always --no-git
</code></pre>
<p><code>--yes-always</code> 플래그로 모든 승인을 자동 수락한다. stdin 파이프라인에서 CI/CD 연동에 사용된다. 별도 JSON 출력 포맷은 없다.</p>
<h3>2.4 File Watcher 모드</h3>
<pre><code class="language-bash">aider --watch-files
</code></pre>
<p><code>FileWatcher</code> 클래스가 파일 변경을 감시하고, <code># aider: ...</code> 주석이 포함된 변경을 자동으로 처리한다.</p>
<h3>2.5 ClipboardWatcher</h3>
<p>클립보드 변경을 감시하여 사용자가 복사한 에러 메시지 등을 자동으로 대화에 주입한다.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. LLM 통합 (LiteLLM)</h2>
<h3>3.1 다중 제공사 지원</h3>
<p>Aider는 LiteLLM을 통해 100+ 모델 제공사를 지원한다. 이것은 Codex(OpenAI 전용)나 Claude Code(Anthropic 전용)와 대비되는 핵심 강점이다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py — 모델 레지스트리
class ModelSettings:
    # 모델별 설정: edit_format, use_repo_map, send_undo_reply, ...

# 모델 선택 우선순위:
#   1. --model CLI 인수
#   2. AIDER_MODEL 환경변수
#   3. 사용 가능한 API 키에서 추론
#   4. OpenRouter OAuth 제안
</code></pre>
<h3>3.2 편집 포맷 전략</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>포맷</th>
<th>클래스</th>
<th>설명</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>diff</code></td>
<td><code>EditBlockCoder</code></td>
<td>SEARCH/REPLACE 블록</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>whole</code></td>
<td><code>WholeCoder</code></td>
<td>전체 파일 대체</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>udiff</code></td>
<td><code>UnifiedDiffCoder</code></td>
<td>unified diff 형식</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>architect</code></td>
<td><code>ArchitectCoder</code></td>
<td>고수준 설계 → 구현으로 2단계 분리</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<h2>4. Git 통합</h2>
<h3>4.1 GitRepo 클래스</h3>
<p><code>GitRepo</code> 클래스가 <code>gitpython</code>을 통해 Git 작업을 관리한다. Aider의 독창적 기능은 <strong>자동 커밋</strong>이다.</p>
<pre><code>자동 커밋 흐름:
  1. LLM이 편집 응답 반환
  2. Coder가 편집 적용
  3. 변경된 파일 자동 스테이징
  4. aider 포맷 커밋 메시지 생성
  5. 자동 커밋 (--auto-commits 기본 활성)
</code></pre>
<h3>4.2 Repo Map</h3>
<p><code>RepoMap</code> 클래스가 저장소 전체의 파일/클래스/함수 맵을 생성하여 LLM에 컨텍스트로 제공한다. tree-sitter를 사용한 AST 기반 분석이다.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. 명령어 시스템</h2>
<h3>5.1 Commands 클래스</h3>
<p><code>/</code> 접두사 없는 자연어 명령과 <code>/</code> 접두사 명령을 모두 처리한다.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>명령어</th>
<th>역할</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>/add</code></td>
<td>파일을 대화 컨텍스트에 추가</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/drop</code></td>
<td>파일을 컨텍스트에서 제거</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/run</code></td>
<td>셸 명령 실행, 출력을 대화에 포함</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/undo</code></td>
<td>마지막 커밋 되돌리기</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/diff</code></td>
<td>마지막 변경 diff 표시</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/clear</code></td>
<td>대화 히스토리 초기화</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/map</code></td>
<td>저장소 맵 표시</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/architect</code></td>
<td>architect 모드로 전환</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/ask</code></td>
<td>편집 없이 질문만</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/lint</code></td>
<td>lint 실행</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>/test</code></td>
<td>테스트 실행</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>5.2 SwitchCoder 패턴</h3>
<p><code>SwitchCoder</code> 예외를 통해 런타임에 Coder 인스턴스를 교체한다. 예를 들어 <code>/architect</code> 명령으로 <code>ArchitectCoder</code>로 전환할 때 사용된다.</p>

<h3>Aider 서피스의 독창적 요소</h3>
<ol>
<li><strong>모델 불가지론</strong>: LiteLLM 덕분에 어떤 LLM 제공사든 연결 가능</li>
<li><strong>편집 포맷 다양성</strong>: 4종 편집 전략으로 모델 특성에 최적화</li>
<li><strong>자동 Git 커밋</strong>: LLM 편집을 자동 커밋하여 되돌리기 용이</li>
<li><strong>Repo Map</strong>: tree-sitter 기반 AST 분석으로 대규모 코드베이스 대응</li>
<li><strong>파일 감시</strong>: 코드가 바뀌면 자동으로 대화에 반영하는 반응형 모드</li>
</ol>
<hr>

<h2>9. WP53 검증 (corpus ≥12 KB)</h2>
<p>WP53(<code>devlog/_plan/260627_cc_src_reanalysis/560_phase53_ai_batch_12kb.md</code>)은 <code>ai</code> T2 prefix 7축 문서를 <strong>≥12,288 bytes</strong>로 맞추는 배치다. 본 문서(<code>06_ai_surface</code>)는 표면 축이므로 아래 항목을 재검증한다.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>검증 항목</th>
<th>소스 앵커</th>
<th>기대</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>진입점 단일 프로세스</td>
<td><code>main.py:main()</code></td>
<td>app-server 프로세스 없음</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CLI 표면</td>
<td><code>io.py:InputOutput.get_input</code></td>
<td>prompt_toolkit 기본</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>GUI 표면</td>
<td><code>gui.py:get_coder</code>, <code>launch_gui</code></td>
<td>Streamlit subprocess</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>파이프 표면</td>
<td><code>--yes-always</code>, <code>self.yes=True</code></td>
<td>비대화형 자동 승인</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LLM 표면</td>
<td><code>models.py:litellm.completion</code></td>
<td>provider 문자열 하나로 라우팅</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>명령 표면</td>
<td><code>commands.py:Commands</code></td>
<td><code>/</code> 슬래시 명령</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Git 표면</td>
<td><code>repo.py:GitRepo</code></td>
<td>gitpython, 자동 커밋</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>검증 명령: <code>wc -c 006_app-server-client-surfaces/06_ai_surface.md</code> ≥ 12288. 경로·플래그는 릴리스마다 drift 가능 — 업그레이드 시 <code>main.py</code> argparse와 <code>gui.py</code> <code>CaptureIO</code> 생성부를 우선 재확인.</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. LiteLLM 다중 제공사 표면</h2>
<p>Aider의 <strong>유일한 원격 LLM 표면</strong>은 LiteLLM 래퍼다. Codex(OpenAI 전용)나 Claude Code(Anthropic 전용)와 달리, 클라이언트는 모델 <strong>문자열</strong> 하나로 100+ backend에 연결한다.</p>
<h3>10.1 표면 계층</h3>
<pre><code>CLI/GUI --model / AIDER_MODEL
    → models.Model (name, edit_format, repo_map flags)
    → models.py:litellm.completion(**kwargs)
    → LiteLLM router (OPENAI_API_KEY, ANTHROPIC_API_KEY, OPENROUTER_API_KEY, …)
    → upstream HTTP
</code></pre>
<h3>10.2 부트스트랩 훅 (<code>main.py</code>)</h3>
<p>순서: <code>register_models</code> → <code>register_litellm_models</code> → <code>select_default_model</code>. API 키가 없으면 <code>onboarding.py</code>가 OpenRouter OAuth를 <code>confirm_ask</code>로 제안한다 — 이것도 표면의 일부(온보딩 프롬프트)다.</p>
<h3>10.3 모델 메타데이터 표면</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>API</th>
<th>역할</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>litellm.get_model_info</code></td>
<td>provider, context window</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>litellm.validate_environment</code></td>
<td>키/엔드포인트 검증</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>litellm.model_cost</code></td>
<td><code>register_litellm_models</code> 비용 테이블</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>litellm.encode</code> / <code>token_counter</code></td>
<td>컨텍스트 예산</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>10.4 제공사별 차이는 모델 설정으로 흡수</h3>
<p><code>ModelSettings</code>가 <code>edit_format</code>, <code>use_repo_map</code>, <code>send_undo_reply</code> 등을 모델별로 분기한다. <strong>wire protocol 차이는 LiteLLM 내부</strong>에 숨고, Aider 클라이언트는 동일한 <code>Coder.send_message</code> 경로만 본다. 프로그래매틱 SDK가 없으므로 외부 통합은 CLI 인수·환경변수·stdin 파이프가 전부다.</p>
<h3>10.5 GUI에서의 모델 표면</h3>
<p><code>gui.py</code>는 <code>cli_main(return_coder=True)</code>로 동일 Coder를 재사용한다. Streamlit 사이드바에서 모델/파일을 바꿀 수 있으나, LLM 호출 경로는 CLI와 동일한 <code>main_model.send_completion</code>이다. 별도 app-server RPC 없음.</p>
<hr>
<h2>11. <code>confirm_ask</code>: CLI vs GUI</h2>
<p>승인 UX는 Codex guardian과 달리 <strong>단일 <code>InputOutput.confirm_ask</code> 구현</strong>을 공유한다(<code>012_guardian-approval/12_ai_guardian.md</code>).</p>
<h3>11.1 CLI (기본)</h3>
<ul>
<li><code>main.py:get_io()</code> → <code>InputOutput(pretty, args.yes_always, …)</code> (<code>554</code>)</li>
<li><code>--yes-always</code> → <code>self.yes=True</code> → 대부분 자동 yes; <strong>shell은 <code>explicit_yes_required</code>로 예외</strong></li>
<li><code>--yes</code> / <code>--no</code>도 <code>self.yes</code> tri-state로 전달</li>
<li>prompt_toolkit <code>PromptSession</code> 또는 plain <code>input</code></li>
</ul>
<h3>11.2 GUI (<code>CaptureIO</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># gui.py:77-84
io = CaptureIO(pretty=False, yes=True, dry_run=coder.io.dry_run, ...)
coder.commands.io = io  # commands 경로만 교체; coder.io는 유지
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li><code>yes=True</code> 고정 → <strong>GUI는 대화형 confirm 없이 자동 승인</strong> (shell 제외: <code>explicit_yes_required</code>)</li>
<li><code>CaptureIO</code>는 <code>tool_output</code>/<code>tool_error</code>/<code>tool_warning</code>만 캡처; <code>confirm_ask</code> 오버라이드 없음</li>
<li>Streamlit은 stdin이 없어 CLI prompt 대신 자동 yes가 실질적 UX</li>
</ul>
<h3>11.3 파이프 / CI</h3>
<p><code>echo … \| aider --yes-always</code> — <code>self.yes=True</code>, non-TTY. guardian/policy 없이 일괄 승인. shell 명령만 사용자 명시 <code>y</code> 필요.</p>
<h3>11.4 표면 관점 함의</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>표면</th>
<th>confirm 동작</th>
<th>프로그래매틱 승인 API</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>CLI 대화형</td>
<td>full prompt</td>
<td>없음</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CLI <code>--yes-always</code></td>
<td>auto yes (shell excepted)</td>
<td>플래그만</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>GUI Streamlit</td>
<td>auto yes (<code>yes=True</code>)</td>
<td>없음</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Codex app-server</td>
<td>JSON-RPC approval events</td>
<td>protocol + SDK</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<h2>12. Parity vs <code>co</code> app-server (<code>06_co_surface.md</code>)</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>차원</th>
<th>Codex <code>co</code></th>
<th>Aider <code>ai</code></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>프로세스 모델</td>
<td>CLI + 장기 실행 <code>app-server</code></td>
<td>단일 Python 프로세스</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Wire protocol</td>
<td>JSON-RPC v2 (<code>app-server-protocol</code>)</td>
<td><strong>없음</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Client facade</td>
<td><code>app-server-client</code> in-process / WebSocket</td>
<td><code>InputOutput</code> + optional Streamlit</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SDK</td>
<td>Rust/Python/TS wrappers</td>
<td><strong>없음</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rich client</td>
<td>VS Code, remote WS</td>
<td>Streamlit 브라우저 탭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>승인 표면</td>
<td>guardian + user approval RPC</td>
<td><code>confirm_ask</code> 터미널/GUI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LLM 표면</td>
<td>OpenAI Codex API</td>
<td>LiteLLM multi-provider</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Thread lifecycle</td>
<td><code>thread/start</code>, <code>thread/resume</code>, fork</td>
<td>Coder 인스턴스 + <code>SwitchCoder</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Transport</td>
<td>stdio://, ws://</td>
<td>stdin/stdout, Streamlit HTTP</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Non-interactive</td>
<td>exec mode, policy profiles</td>
<td><code>--yes-always</code>, GUI <code>yes=True</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>추출 seam 관점</strong>: Codex 포크는 <code>app-server-protocol</code>부터; Aider 참조는 <strong>LiteLLM 모델 문자열 + Coder 편집 전략 + Repo Map</strong>이지 서버 프로토콜이 아니다. jaw/cli-jaw류 제품이 Aider式 단일 프로세스를 택하면 app-server 삼각형 전체가 불필요하고, Codex式 rich client를 택하면 Aider Streamlit GUI는 wire events를 대체하지 못한다.</p>
<h3>12.1 공통점 (얕은)</h3>
<ul>
<li>둘 다 대화형 코딩 에이전트</li>
<li>shell 실행 전 사용자 게이트 존재 (co: guardian+user, ai: <code>confirm_ask</code>)</li>
<li>Git 워크플로 통합 (co: 도구, ai: 자동 커밋 내장)</li>
</ul>
<h3>12.2 비목표 (Aider가 co app-server를 대체하지 않는 영역)</h3>
<ul>
<li>IDE 확장용 JSON-RPC notification stream</li>
<li>Remote WebSocket multi-client</li>
<li>Thread archive/rollback wire API</li>
<li>Structured approval request schema</li>
</ul>

<h2>변경 기록</h2>
<ul>

<li>2026-03-26: Aider 앱서버/클라이언트 서피스를 오픈소스 분석. 서피스 부재를 핵심 특성으로 정리. CLI/Streamlit GUI/파이프 모드 3가지 표면, LiteLLM 다중 제공사, 4종 편집 전략, 자동 Git 커밋, Repo Map, 5개 에이전트 비교를 포함.</li>

1b:["$","$L28","20-axis-06-surface",{"id":"20-axis-06-surface","order":23,"tier":"deep","title":"축 06: 앱·서버 표면","description":"006_app-server-client-surfaces/06_ai_surface.md","lang":"ko","badge":"AXIS","children":["$","div",null,{"dangerouslySetInnerHTML":{"__html":"$3b"}}]}]
3c:T71de,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>Aider executes model-suggested commands and user <code>/run</code> invocations in the <strong>real user shell</strong> with working directory <code>self.root</code> (git project root). Safety relies on <strong>explicit human confirmation</strong>, not capability restriction. This is fundamentally different from Codex's sandbox policy engine and seatbelt profiles documented in <code>07_co_sandbox.md</code>.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>Executive summary</li>
<li>Architecture — execution flow</li>
<li>No OS sandbox — negative evidence</li>
<li><code>run_shell_commands</code> — post-edit execution loop</li>
<li>Entry and early exit</li>
<li>Call site in edit pipeline</li>
<li><code>handle_shell_commands</code> — confirmation contract</li>
<li><code>ConfirmGroup</code> — batch confirmation primitive</li>
<li><code>confirm_ask</code> — interactive gate implementation</li>
<li>Shell line extraction — <code>EditBlockCoder</code></li>
<li><code>run_cmd.py</code> — host execution engine</li>
<li>Top-level router</li>
</ul>
<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">sequenceDiagram
    participant LLM as Model response
    participant EB as EditBlockCoder
    participant BC as base_coder
    participant IO as InputOutput
    participant CG as ConfirmGroup
    participant RC as run_cmd.py
    participant SH as Host shell

    LLM->>EB: edit blocks + shell lines
    EB->>BC: shell_commands += lines
    BC->>BC: apply_edits / auto_lint
    BC->>BC: run_shell_commands()
    BC->>CG: ConfirmGroup(commands)
    BC->>IO: confirm_ask Run shell command?
    IO-->>BC: yes / no / all / never
    BC->>RC: run_cmd(cmd, cwd=root)
    RC->>SH: subprocess or pexpect
    SH-->>RC: stdout + exit code
    RC-->>BC: output
    BC->>IO: Add output to chat?
    IO-->>BC: optional inject cur_messages
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">def run_shell_commands(self):
    if not self.suggest_shell_commands:
        return ""

    done = set()
    group = ConfirmGroup(set(self.shell_commands))
    accumulated_output = ""
    for command in self.shell_commands:
        if command in done:
            continue
        done.add(command)
        output = self.handle_shell_commands(command, group)
        if output:
            accumulated_output += output + "\n\n"
    return accumulated_output
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">shared_output = self.run_shell_commands()
if shared_output:
    self.cur_messages += [
        dict(role="user", content=shared_output),
        dict(role="assistant", content="Ok"),
    ]
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">def handle_shell_commands(self, commands_str, group):
    commands = commands_str.strip().splitlines()
    command_count = sum(
        1 for cmd in commands if cmd.strip() and not cmd.strip().startswith("#")
    )
    prompt = "Run shell command?" if command_count == 1 else "Run shell commands?"
    if not self.io.confirm_ask(
        prompt,
        subject="\n".join(commands),
        explicit_yes_required=True,
        group=group,
        allow_never=True,
    ):
        return

    accumulated_output = ""
    for command in commands:
        command = command.strip()
        if not command or command.startswith("#"):
            continue

        self.io.tool_output(f"Running {command}")
        self.io.add_to_input_history(f"/run {command.strip()}")
        exit_status, output = run_cmd(command, error_print=self.io.tool_error, cwd=self.root)
        if output:
            accumulated_output += f"Output from {command}\n{output}\n"

    if accumulated_output.strip() and self.io.confirm_ask(
        "Add command output to the chat?", allow_never=True
    ):
        ...
        return accumulated_output
</code></pre>

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">def run_cmd_pexpect(command, verbose=False, cwd=None):
    shell = os.environ.get("SHELL", "/bin/sh")
    if os.path.exists(shell):
        child = pexpect.spawn(shell, args=["-i", "-c", command], encoding="utf-8", cwd=cwd)
    else:
        child = pexpect.spawn(command, encoding="utf-8", cwd=cwd)
    child.interact(output_filter=output_callback)
    child.close()
    return child.exitstatus, output.getvalue().decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
</code></pre>

<h2>코퍼스 — 007_sandbox-exec-policy/07_ai_sandbox.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Aider Sandbox / Exec Policy</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>110_aider/</code> — <strong>no OS sandbox</strong> (no seatbelt, container, or syscall filter). Shell execution uses <strong><code>run_cmd()</code></strong> on the host with interactive <strong><code>confirm_ask</code></strong> gates and <strong><code>ConfirmGroup</code></strong> batching.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Aider executes model-suggested commands and user <code>/run</code> invocations in the <strong>real user shell</strong> with working directory <code>self.root</code> (git project root). Safety relies on <strong>explicit human confirmation</strong>, not capability restriction. This is fundamentally different from Codex's sandbox policy engine and seatbelt profiles documented in <code>07_co_sandbox.md</code>.</p>
<p>This document traces the full execution path: shell line extraction from edits → confirmation UI → <code>run_cmd.py</code> subprocess/pexpect → optional chat injection — and documents deliberate absences (no allowlist classifier, no network policy, no filesystem jail).</p>
<h2>Executive summary</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Policy surface</th>
<th>Behavior</th>
<th>Citation</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>OS sandbox</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
<td>corpus audit — no seatbelt/docker/nsjail</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Model-suggested shell</td>
<td><code>run_shell_commands()</code> after edits</td>
<td><code>base_coder.py:2434-2485</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>User <code>/run</code></td>
<td>Immediate <code>run_cmd</code>, then token confirm</td>
<td><code>commands.py:1013-1053</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Confirmation</td>
<td><code>confirm_ask(explicit_yes_required=True)</code> for shell batches</td>
<td><code>base_coder.py:2456-2461</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Batch dedup</td>
<td><code>ConfirmGroup(set(shell_commands))</code></td>

</tr>

<td><code>/test</code> → <code>cmd_run</code> on non-zero exit</td>

</table>
<h2>Architecture — execution flow</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">sequenceDiagram
    participant LLM as Model response
    participant EB as EditBlockCoder
    participant BC as base_coder
    participant IO as InputOutput
    participant CG as ConfirmGroup
    participant RC as run_cmd.py
    participant SH as Host shell

    LLM->>EB: edit blocks + shell lines
    EB->>BC: shell_commands += lines
    BC->>BC: apply_edits / auto_lint
    BC->>BC: run_shell_commands()
    BC->>CG: ConfirmGroup(commands)
    BC->>IO: confirm_ask Run shell command?
    IO-->>BC: yes / no / all / never
    BC->>RC: run_cmd(cmd, cwd=root)
    RC->>SH: subprocess or pexpect
    SH-->>RC: stdout + exit code
    RC-->>BC: output
    BC->>IO: Add output to chat?
    IO-->>BC: optional inject cur_messages
</code></pre>
<p>User-initiated <code>/run</code> skips the edit-block collection step but shares <code>run_cmd()</code> and similar output injection policy.</p>
<h2>No OS sandbox — negative evidence</h2>
<p>Search under <code>110_aider/aider/</code> for seatbelt, sandbox profiles, <code>nsjail</code>, <code>bubblewrap</code>, dockerized exec, or syscall filtering returns <strong>no enforcement layer</strong>. Execution always delegates to:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>subprocess.Popen(..., shell=True)</code> (<code>run_cmd.py:62-73</code>), or</li>
<li><code>pexpect.spawn(shell, args=["-i", "-c", command])</code> (<code>run_cmd.py:116-121</code>).</li>
</ul>
<p>There is no step that wraps commands in macOS <code>sandbox-exec</code>, Linux namespaces, or WASM isolation. <strong>Policy = ask the user.</strong></p>
<p>Contrast Codex (<code>co</code>): policy engine + guardian + optional seatbelt before spawn.</p>
<h2><code>run_shell_commands</code> — post-edit execution loop</h2>
<h3>Entry and early exit</h3>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/coders/base_coder.py:2434-2448</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def run_shell_commands(self):
    if not self.suggest_shell_commands:
        return ""

    done = set()
    group = ConfirmGroup(set(self.shell_commands))
    accumulated_output = ""
    for command in self.shell_commands:
        if command in done:
            continue
        done.add(command)
        output = self.handle_shell_commands(command, group)
        if output:
            accumulated_output += output + "\n\n"
    return accumulated_output
</code></pre>
<p>Gate: class default <code>suggest_shell_commands = True</code> (<code>base_coder.py:117</code>); constructor stores flag (<code>364</code>); CLI passes <code>args.suggest_shell_commands</code> (<code>main.py:1000</code>).</p>
<p>When disabled, system prompt uses <code>no_shell_cmd_prompt</code> instead of shell encouragement (<code>base_coder.py:1187-1196</code>).</p>
<h3>Call site in edit pipeline</h3>
<p>After lint, before auto-test — <code>base_coder.py:1609-1614</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">shared_output = self.run_shell_commands()
if shared_output:
    self.cur_messages += [
        dict(role="user", content=shared_output),
        dict(role="assistant", content="Ok"),
    ]
</code></pre>
<p>Shell output becomes <strong>chat context</strong> for the next model turn if user confirms injection inside <code>handle_shell_commands</code>.</p>
<h2><code>handle_shell_commands</code> — confirmation contract</h2>
<p><code>base_coder.py:2450-2485</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def handle_shell_commands(self, commands_str, group):
    commands = commands_str.strip().splitlines()
    command_count = sum(
        1 for cmd in commands if cmd.strip() and not cmd.strip().startswith("#")
    )
    prompt = "Run shell command?" if command_count == 1 else "Run shell commands?"
    if not self.io.confirm_ask(
        prompt,
        subject="\n".join(commands),
        explicit_yes_required=True,
        group=group,
        allow_never=True,
    ):
        return

    accumulated_output = ""
    for command in commands:
        command = command.strip()
        if not command or command.startswith("#"):
            continue

        self.io.tool_output(f"Running {command}")
        self.io.add_to_input_history(f"/run {command.strip()}")
        exit_status, output = run_cmd(command, error_print=self.io.tool_error, cwd=self.root)
        if output:
            accumulated_output += f"Output from {command}\n{output}\n"

    if accumulated_output.strip() and self.io.confirm_ask(
        "Add command output to the chat?", allow_never=True
    ):
        ...
        return accumulated_output
</code></pre>
<p>Policy knobs:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parameter</th>
<th>Effect</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>explicit_yes_required=True</code></td>
<td>User must actively confirm — no default-yes for shell</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>group=group</code></td>
<td>Enables All/Skip batch answers via ConfirmGroup</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>allow_never=True</code></td>
<td>"Don't ask again" stores in <code>never_prompts</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>#</code> lines</td>
<td>Treated as comments, skipped</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cwd=self.root</code></td>
<td>Runs relative to git project root, not arbitrary</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Not present:</strong> command allowlist, denylist regex, max runtime kill, network block, output size cap before run (only token estimate on <code>/run</code> add-to-chat).</p>
<h2><code>ConfirmGroup</code> — batch confirmation primitive</h2>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/io.py:81-88</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">@dataclass
class ConfirmGroup:
    preference: str = None
    show_group: bool = True

    def __init__(self, items=None):
        if items is not None:
            self.show_group = len(items) > 1
</code></pre>
<p>When multiple distinct shell commands are queued, <code>show_group=True</code> exposes <code>(A)ll</code> / <code>(S)kip all</code> in <code>confirm_ask</code> (<code>io.py:833-836</code>). Single-command batches hide group shortcuts (<code>826-827</code>).</p>
<p>Same primitive used for:</p>
<ul>
<li>URL fetches — <code>base_coder.py:972</code></li>
<li>File mention adds — <code>base_coder.py:1770</code></li>
<li>Shell commands — <code>base_coder.py:2439</code></li>
</ul>
<p>This is UX batching, <strong>not</strong> a security boundary.</p>
<h2><code>confirm_ask</code> — interactive gate implementation</h2>
<p><code>io.py:807-846</code> signature:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def confirm_ask(
    self,
    question,
    default="y",
    subject=None,
    explicit_yes_required=False,
    group=None,
    allow_never=False,
):
</code></pre>
<p>Shell uses <code>explicit_yes_required=True</code> — stricter than lint fix prompts (<code>commands.py:389</code> uses <code>default="y"</code> without explicit_yes).</p>
<p><code>never_prompts</code> set (<code>io.py:823-824</code>) permanently skips categories user rejects with "Don't ask again" — session-persistent preference, not a global exec policy file.</p>
<h2>Shell line extraction — <code>EditBlockCoder</code></h2>
<p>Model places shell commands in special edit blocks. <code>110_aider/aider/coders/editblock_coder.py:21-36</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def get_edits(self):
    content = self.partial_response_content
    edits = list(find_original_update_blocks(...))
    self.shell_commands += [edit[1] for edit in edits if edit[0] is None]
    edits = [edit for edit in edits if edit[0] is not None]
    return edits
</code></pre>
<p>Tuples with <code>edit[0] is None</code> are shell directives, not file patches. They accumulate in <code>self.shell_commands</code> initialized empty each turn (<code>base_coder.py:407</code>, cleared <code>870</code>).</p>
<p>Other coder formats may not extract shell lines — behavior is format-specific.</p>
<h2><code>run_cmd.py</code> — host execution engine</h2>
<h3>Top-level router</h3>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/run_cmd.py:11-23</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def run_cmd(command, verbose=False, error_print=None, cwd=None):
    try:
        if sys.stdin.isatty() and hasattr(pexpect, "spawn") and platform.system() != "Windows":
            return run_cmd_pexpect(command, verbose, cwd)
        return run_cmd_subprocess(command, verbose, cwd)
    except OSError as e:
        ...
        return 1, error_message
</code></pre>
<p><strong>TTY + non-Windows</strong> → interactive <code>pexpect</code> path (user can interact mid-command). Otherwise → subprocess capture.</p>
<h3>Subprocess path — <code>shell=True</code></h3>
<p><code>run_cmd.py:42-84</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def run_cmd_subprocess(command, verbose=False, cwd=None, encoding=sys.stdout.encoding):
    ...
    if platform.system() == "Windows":
        parent_process = get_windows_parent_process_name()
        if parent_process == "powershell.exe":
            command = f"powershell -Command {command}"

    process = subprocess.Popen(
        command,
        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
        stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
        text=True,
        shell=True,
        encoding=encoding,
        errors="replace",
        bufsize=0,
        universal_newlines=True,
        cwd=cwd,
    )
    ...
    process.wait()
    return process.returncode, "".join(output)
</code></pre>
<p>Implications:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong><code>shell=True</code></strong> — full shell metacharacter interpretation; injection risk if model suggests malicious commands and user approves.</li>
<li><strong>Real-time stdout</strong> printed to terminal during read loop (<code>80</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Windows</strong> may wrap in PowerShell when parent is powershell.exe (<code>51-54</code>).</li>
<li><strong>No timeout</strong> — long-running commands block until exit.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Pexpect path — interactive shell</h3>
<p><code>run_cmd.py:89-128</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def run_cmd_pexpect(command, verbose=False, cwd=None):
    shell = os.environ.get("SHELL", "/bin/sh")
    if os.path.exists(shell):
        child = pexpect.spawn(shell, args=["-i", "-c", command], encoding="utf-8", cwd=cwd)
    else:
        child = pexpect.spawn(command, encoding="utf-8", cwd=cwd)
    child.interact(output_filter=output_callback)
    child.close()
    return child.exitstatus, output.getvalue().decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
</code></pre>
<p>Uses user's <code>$SHELL</code> — typically bash/zsh with full user profile. <strong><code>interact</code></strong> hands keyboard to subprocess — even less isolated than headless capture.</p>
<h3>Shared with linter</h3>
<p><code>linter.py:15</code> imports <code>run_cmd_subprocess</code> for lint commands — same execution stack, same lack of sandbox (<code>linter.py:53-57</code>).</p>
<h2><code>/run</code> slash command — user-initiated exec</h2>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/commands.py:1013-1053</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def cmd_run(self, args, add_on_nonzero_exit=False):

        args, verbose=self.verbose, error_print=self.io.tool_error, cwd=self.coder.root
    )
    ...

    k_tokens = token_count / 1000

    if add_on_nonzero_exit:
        add = exit_status != 0

        add = self.io.confirm_ask(f"Add {k_tokens:.1f}k tokens of command output to the chat?")

<p>Bang alias: <code>commands.py:313-315</code> — <code>!cmd</code> → <code>do_run("run", inp[1:])</code>.</p>
<h3><code>/test</code> wrapper</h3>
<p><code>commands.py:993-1004</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def cmd_test(self, args):
    ...
    return self.cmd_run(args, True)
</code></pre>
<p>Auto-adds output on non-zero exit — used by <code>auto_test</code> loop (<code>base_coder.py:1616-1623</code>).</p>
<h2>Architect mode — shell disabled on editor pass</h2>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/coders/architect_coder.py:25-27</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">kwargs["suggest_shell_commands"] = False
</code></pre>
<p>Architect model plans; editor model applies patches <strong>without</strong> being prompted to suggest shell. Reduces accidental command execution during file-edit phase — policy by <strong>coder subclass</strong>, not sandbox.</p>
<h2>Git operations — separate confirm surface</h2>
<p>Git commits, dirty commits before edits, and <code>/commit</code> follow repo-aware flows in <code>commands.py</code> and <code>base_coder.py</code> (<code>dirty_commit</code> at <code>2411-2423</code>). These are version-control policies, not syscall sandboxing.</p>
<h2>Prompt-level "policy" — not enforcement</h2>
<p>When <code>suggest_shell_commands=True</code>, system prompt includes <code>shell_cmd_prompt</code> and reminders (<code>base_coder.py:1187-1189</code>) telling the model how to format shell blocks. When False, <code>no_shell_cmd_prompt</code> discourages shell suggestions (<code>1192-1195</code>).</p>
<p><strong>Prompt text is not enforcement</strong> — a non-compliant model could still emit shell blocks collected by <code>EditBlockCoder</code>, but user must confirm execution.</p>
<h2>Threat model summary</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Risk</th>
<th>Mitigation in Aider</th>
<th>Codex-style mitigation</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Arbitrary shell</td>
<td>User confirm (explicit yes)</td>
<td>Sandbox + policy + guardian</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Filesystem wipe</td>
<td>None — full user permissions</td>
<td>Seatbelt write restrictions</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Network exfil</td>
<td>None — commands can curl freely</td>
<td>Network policy / sandbox</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Long-running fork bomb</td>
<td>No timeout</td>
<td>Process limits / cgroup</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Supply-chain in command</td>
<td>User responsibility</td>
<td>Allowlist classifiers</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Aider assumes a <strong>trusted user</strong> approving commands in their own dev environment.</p>
<h2>Comparison table — exec policy</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Concern</th>
<th><code>co</code> (Codex)</th>
<th><code>ai</code> (Aider)</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>OS sandbox</td>
<td>seatbelt / policy engine</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Exec gate</td>
<td>policy + guardian</td>
<td><code>confirm_ask</code> only</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CWD</td>
<td>sandbox root</td>
<td><code>self.root</code> git root</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>shell=True</td>
<td>Controlled spawn</td>
<td>Always in <code>run_cmd_subprocess</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCP tool timeout</td>
<td><code>tool_timeout_sec</code></td>
<td><strong>None</strong> for shell</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Batch confirm</td>
<td>N/A (policy decides)</td>
<td><code>ConfirmGroup</code></td>
</tr>

<h2>Operational guidance</h2>
<h3>Disable model-suggested shell</h3>
<p>Launch with <code>--no-suggest-shell-commands</code> (see <code>args.py</code> / main wiring <code>main.py:1000</code>). Editor pass in architect mode already disables via <code>architect_coder.py:27</code>.</p>
<h3>Safer workflows (user-operated)</h3>
<ul>
<li>Run Aider in a disposable VM or container <strong>externally</strong> — Aider won't containerize for you.</li>
<li>Use git snapshots / <code>dirty_commits</code> so file state is recoverable before risky approves.</li>
<li>Prefer <code>/run</code> manually instead of approving model-suggested batches when uncertain.</li>
</ul>

1c:["$","$L28","20-axis-07-sandbox",{"id":"20-axis-07-sandbox","order":24,"tier":"deep","title":"축 07: 샌드박스·정책","description":"007_sandbox-exec-policy/07_ai_sandbox.md","lang":"ko","badge":"AXIS","children":["$","div",null,{"dangerouslySetInnerHTML":{"__html":"$3c"}}]}]
3d:T9bbd,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>Aider의 설정은 <strong>configargparse</strong> 기반의 3계층 병합 구조다. CLI 인자 → YAML 설정 파일 → 환경변수(<code>AIDER_</code> 접두사) 순으로 우선순위가 정해지며, 모델 메타데이터는 별도 파이프라인으로 로드된다. configargparse가 argparse를 확장하여 YAML 파일과 환경변수를 동일 네임스페이스에 자동 병합하는 점이 핵심이다.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>기술 참조</li>
<li>CLI 인자 시스템 (args.py)</li>
<li>설정 파일 탐색 로직</li>
<li>환경변수 자동 매핑</li>
<li>.env 파일 로딩</li>
<li><code>generate_search_path_list()</code> — 공통 파일 탐색</li>
<li>모델 관리 시스템 (models.py)</li>
<li>ModelSettings 데이터클래스</li>
<li>Model 초기화 파이프라인</li>
<li>모델 설정 해결 순서 <code>configure_model_settings()</code></li>
<li><code>apply_generic_model_settings()</code> — 패턴 매칭 상세</li>
<li>ModelInfoManager — 4단계 메타데이터 파이프라인</li>
</ul>

default_config_files = []
default_config_files += [conf_fname.resolve()]       # CWD
if git_root:
    git_conf = Path(git_root) / conf_fname            # git root

# 1차 파싱 후 역순으로 재정렬하여 2차 파싱

def load_dotenv_files(git_root, dotenv_fname, encoding="utf-8"):
    dotenv_files = generate_search_path_list(".env", git_root, dotenv_fname)
    oauth_keys_file = Path.home() / ".aider" / "oauth-keys.env"
    if oauth_keys_file.exists():
        dotenv_files.insert(0, str(oauth_keys_file.resolve()))
    for fname in dotenv_files:
        if Path(fname).exists():
            load_dotenv(fname, override=True, encoding=encoding)

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/main.py:305-332
def generate_search_path_list(default_file, git_root, command_line_file):
    files = []
    files.append(Path.home() / default_file)   # 1. HOME
    if git_root:
        files.append(Path(git_root) / default_file)  # 2. git root
    files.append(default_file)                  # 3. CWD
    if command_line_file:
        files.append(command_line_file)          # 4. CLI 지정 파일 (최우선)
    files.reverse()  # 우선순위 역전 → CLI > CWD > git root > HOME
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:421-583 — 주요 패턴 규칙 (실제 소스 코드)
def apply_generic_model_settings(self, model):
    # 1. o3-mini: diff + repo_map + reasoning_effort
    if "/o3-mini" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.use_temperature = False
        self.system_prompt_prefix = "Formatting re-enabled. "
        if "reasoning_effort" not in self.accepts_settings:
            self.accepts_settings.append("reasoning_effort")
        return

    # 2. gpt-4.1-mini: diff + repo_map
    if "gpt-4.1-mini" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.reminder = "sys"
        return

    # 3. gpt-5: diff + reasoning_effort + no temperature
    last_segment = model.split("/")[-1]
    if last_segment in ("gpt-5", "gpt-5-2025-08-07"):
        self.use_temperature = False
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        if "reasoning_effort" not in self.accepts_settings:
            self.accepts_settings.append("reasoning_effort")
        return

    # 4. deepseek v3: diff + repo_map + sys examples
    if "deepseek" in model and "v3" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.reminder = "sys"
        self.examples_as_sys_msg = True
        return

    # 5. deepseek reasoning (r1): diff + reasoning_tag="think"
    if "deepseek" in model and ("r1" in model or "reasoning" in model):
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.use_temperature = False
        self.reasoning_tag = "think"
        return

    # 6. Claude 4.5/4.6: diff + thinking_tokens
    if "sonnet-4-5" in model or "opus-4-6" in model or "haiku-4-5" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.examples_as_sys_msg = False
        if "thinking_tokens" not in self.accepts_settings:
            self.accepts_settings.append("thinking_tokens")
        return

    # 7. qwq-32b: diff + reasoning_tag="think" + temperature=0.6
    if "qwq" in model and "32b" in model and "preview" not in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.reasoning_tag = "think"
        self.use_temperature = 0.6
        self.extra_params = dict(top_p=0.95)
        return

    # 8. qwen3-235b: diff + /no_think prefix + top_k=20
    if "qwen3" in model and "235b" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.system_prompt_prefix = "/no_think"
        self.use_temperature = 0.7
        self.extra_params = {"top_p": 0.8, "top_k": 20, "min_p": 0.0}
        return

    # ... 15+ 추가 규칙 (llama3-70b, gpt-4-turbo, claude-3-opus 등)
</code></pre>

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:237-262 — 4단계 해석 (실제 소스 코드)
def get_model_info(self, model):
    # ① 사용자 로컬 메타데이터 (최우선)
    cached_info = self.get_model_from_cached_json_db(model)

    # ② litellm 내장 DB (lazy import 최적화)
    litellm_info = None
    if litellm._lazy_module or not cached_info:
        try:
            litellm_info = litellm.get_model_info(model)
        except Exception: pass

    if litellm_info:
        return litellm_info

    # ③ OpenRouter 전용 fallback
    if not cached_info and model.startswith("openrouter/"):
        # 로컬 API 캐시
        openrouter_info = self.openrouter_manager.get_model_info(model)
        if openrouter_info:
            return openrouter_info
        # ④ 웹 스크래핑 (최후 수단)
        openrouter_info = self.fetch_openrouter_model_info(model)
        if openrouter_info:
            return openrouter_info

    return cached_info
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:264-308 — 웹 스크래핑 (실제 소스 코드)
def fetch_openrouter_model_info(self, model):
    url_part = model[len("openrouter/"):]
    url = "https://openrouter.ai/" + url_part
    response = requests.get(url, timeout=5)
    html = response.text
    text = re.sub(r"&#x3C;[^>]+>", " ", html)  # HTML 태그 제거
    # 정규식으로 context, input/output 비용 추출
    context_match = re.search(r"([\d,]+)\s*context", text)
    input_cost_match = re.search(r"\$\s*([\d.]+)\s*/M input tokens", text)
    output_cost_match = re.search(r"\$\s*([\d.]+)\s*/M output tokens", text)
    # ...파싱 결과를 dict으로 반환
</code></pre>

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:697-726 (실제 소스 코드)
def fast_validate_environment(self):
    """litellm import를 강제하지 않는 빠른 경로"""
    model = self.name
    pieces = model.split("/")
    provider = pieces[0] if len(pieces) > 1 else None

    keymap = dict(
        openrouter="OPENROUTER_API_KEY",
        openai="OPENAI_API_KEY",
        deepseek="DEEPSEEK_API_KEY",
        gemini="GEMINI_API_KEY",
        anthropic="ANTHROPIC_API_KEY",
        groq="GROQ_API_KEY",
        fireworks_ai="FIREWORKS_API_KEY",
    )

    # 하드코딩된 모델 목록으로 provider 매핑
    if model in OPENAI_MODELS:
        var = "OPENAI_API_KEY"
    elif model in ANTHROPIC_MODELS:
        var = "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY"
    else:
        var = keymap.get(provider)

    if var and os.environ.get(var):
        return dict(keys_in_environment=[var], missing_keys=[])
    # None 반환 → 느린 경로(litellm.validate_environment)로 fallback
</code></pre>

    MAIN --> EDITOR["editor_model&#x3C;br/>(코드 편집 전용)"]
    WEAK --> WMNAME["weak_model_name&#x3C;br/>ModelSettings에서 결정"]

</code></pre>
<h2>코퍼스 — 008_config-system/08_ai_config.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Aider 설정 시스템 분석</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>110_aider/</code> — configuration system.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Aider의 설정은 <strong>configargparse</strong> 기반의 3계층 병합 구조다. CLI 인자 → YAML 설정 파일 → 환경변수(<code>AIDER_</code> 접두사) 순으로 우선순위가 정해지며, 모델 메타데이터는 별도 파이프라인으로 로드된다. configargparse가 argparse를 확장하여 YAML 파일과 환경변수를 동일 네임스페이스에 자동 병합하는 점이 핵심이다.</p>
<p>설정 우선순위(위가 높음):</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>CLI 인자</strong> — 직접 전달되는 <code>--flag</code> 값</li>
<li><strong>YAML 설정 파일</strong> — <code>.aider.conf.yml</code> (CWD → git root → <code>$HOME</code> 순 탐색)</li>
<li><strong>환경변수</strong> — <code>AIDER_</code> 접두사 자동 매핑 (<code>--model</code> → <code>AIDER_MODEL</code>)</li>
<li><strong>.env 파일</strong> — <code>dotenv</code> 로드 후 재파싱</li>
</ol>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A[".aider.conf.yml&#x3C;br/>(CWD → git root → HOME)"] --> E["configargparse.ArgumentParser"]
    B["CLI args&#x3C;br/>(--model, --dark-mode 등)"] --> E
    C["환경변수&#x3C;br/>(AIDER_ 접두사)"] --> E
    D[".env 파일&#x3C;br/>(dotenv 로드)"] -->|재파싱| E
    E --> F["args Namespace"]

    G["model-settings.yml&#x3C;br/>(패키지 리소스)"] --> H["MODEL_SETTINGS 리스트"]
    I[".aider.model.settings.yml&#x3C;br/>(사용자 오버라이드)"] --> H
    J["model-metadata.json&#x3C;br/>(패키지 리소스)"] --> K["ModelInfoManager"]
    L[".aider.model.metadata.json&#x3C;br/>(사용자 오버라이드)"] --> K
    M["litellm 원격 DB&#x3C;br/>(24h 캐시)"] --> K

    F --> N["Model 인스턴스 생성"]
    H --> N
    K --> N
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>기술 참조</h2>
<h3>CLI 인자 시스템 (args.py)</h3>
<p><code>get_parser()</code> 함수가 <code>configargparse.ArgumentParser</code>를 생성하고, 16개의 <code>add_argument_group()</code>으로 인자를 분류한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/args.py:36-42
parser = configargparse.ArgumentParser(
    description="aider is AI pair programming in your terminal",
    add_config_file_help=True,
    default_config_files=default_config_files,
    config_file_parser_class=configargparse.YAMLConfigFileParser,
    auto_env_var_prefix="AIDER_",
)
</code></pre>

<h3>설정 파일 탐색 로직</h3>
<p><code>main()</code> 함수에서 <code>.aider.conf.yml</code>의 탐색 경로를 조립한다. 역순 재파싱으로 우선순위를 CWD > git root > HOME 순으로 보장한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/main.py:464-496
conf_fname = Path(".aider.conf.yml")
default_config_files = []
default_config_files += [conf_fname.resolve()]       # CWD
if git_root:
    git_conf = Path(git_root) / conf_fname            # git root
    if git_conf not in default_config_files:
        default_config_files.append(git_conf)
default_config_files.append(Path.home() / conf_fname) # HOME

# 1차 파싱 후 역순으로 재정렬하여 2차 파싱
default_config_files.reverse()
parser = get_parser(default_config_files, git_root)
args = parser.parse_args(argv)
</code></pre>
<p>configargparse는 <code>default_config_files</code> 리스트의 <strong>마지막</strong> 파일이 가장 높은 우선순위를 갖는다. 역순 후 재파싱하는 이유가 여기에 있다. CWD의 설정이 HOME보다 우선한다.</p>
<h3>환경변수 자동 매핑</h3>
<p><code>auto_env_var_prefix="AIDER_"</code> 설정으로 모든 CLI 인자가 환경변수로 자동 대응된다:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>--model</code> → <code>AIDER_MODEL</code></li>
<li><code>--dark-mode</code> → <code>AIDER_DARK_MODE</code></li>
<li><code>--auto-commits</code> → <code>AIDER_AUTO_COMMITS</code></li>
</ul>
<p>별도로 <code>--set-env ENV_VAR=value</code> 옵션으로 임의의 환경변수를 주입할 수 있고, <code>--api-key PROVIDER=KEY</code> 는 내부적으로 <code>PROVIDER_API_KEY</code> 환경변수로 변환된다.</p>
<h3>.env 파일 로딩</h3>
<p><code>.env</code> 파일은 <code>generate_search_path_list()</code> 유틸로 탐색되며, OAuth 키 파일(<code>~/.aider/oauth-keys.env</code>)이 최우선으로 로드된다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/main.py:361-387
def load_dotenv_files(git_root, dotenv_fname, encoding="utf-8"):
    dotenv_files = generate_search_path_list(".env", git_root, dotenv_fname)
    oauth_keys_file = Path.home() / ".aider" / "oauth-keys.env"
    if oauth_keys_file.exists():
        dotenv_files.insert(0, str(oauth_keys_file.resolve()))
    for fname in dotenv_files:
        if Path(fname).exists():
            load_dotenv(fname, override=True, encoding=encoding)
</code></pre>
<p><code>.env</code> 로드 후 <code>parser.parse_args(argv)</code>를 <strong>재호출</strong>하여 <code>.env</code>에서 설정된 <code>AIDER_*</code> 환경변수가 args로 반영된다.</p>
<h3><code>generate_search_path_list()</code> — 공통 파일 탐색</h3>
<p>설정 파일, 모델 설정 파일, <code>.env</code> 파일 모두 동일한 탐색 패턴을 따른다:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/main.py:305-332
def generate_search_path_list(default_file, git_root, command_line_file):
    files = []
    files.append(Path.home() / default_file)   # 1. HOME
    if git_root:
        files.append(Path(git_root) / default_file)  # 2. git root
    files.append(default_file)                  # 3. CWD
    if command_line_file:
        files.append(command_line_file)          # 4. CLI 지정 파일 (최우선)
    files.reverse()  # 우선순위 역전 → CLI > CWD > git root > HOME
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>모델 관리 시스템 (models.py)</h2>
<h3>ModelSettings 데이터클래스</h3>
<p>모델별 동작 파라미터를 정의하는 핵심 데이터 구조다. 패키지 리소스의 <code>model-settings.yml</code>에서 초기 로드된 뒤, 사용자의 <code>.aider.model.settings.yml</code>로 오버라이드된다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:115-138
@dataclass
class ModelSettings:
    name: str
    edit_format: str = "whole"
    weak_model_name: Optional[str] = None
    use_repo_map: bool = False
    send_undo_reply: bool = False
    lazy: bool = False
    overeager: bool = False
    reminder: str = "user"
    examples_as_sys_msg: bool = False
    extra_params: Optional[dict] = None
    cache_control: bool = False
    caches_by_default: bool = False
    use_system_prompt: bool = True
    use_temperature: Union[bool, float] = True
    streaming: bool = True
    editor_model_name: Optional[str] = None
    editor_edit_format: Optional[str] = None
    reasoning_tag: Optional[str] = None
    remove_reasoning: Optional[str] = None  # Deprecated alias for reasoning_tag
    system_prompt_prefix: Optional[str] = None
    accepts_settings: Optional[list] = None
</code></pre>
<h3>Model 초기화 파이프라인</h3>
<p><code>Model.__init__()</code>이 모델 인스턴스를 생성하는 전체 흐름:</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A["Model.__init__(model_name)"] --> B["MODEL_ALIASES.get(model)&#x3C;br/>별칭 해석"]
    B --> C["get_model_info(model)&#x3C;br/>ModelInfoManager에서 메타데이터"]
    C --> D["validate_environment()&#x3C;br/>API 키 검증"]
    D --> E["max_chat_history_tokens 계산&#x3C;br/>max_input_tokens / 16&#x3C;br/>min 1024, max 8192"]
    E --> F["configure_model_settings(model)"]
    F --> G["get_weak_model(weak_model)"]
    G --> H["get_editor_model(editor_model)"]
    H --> I["완성된 Model 인스턴스"]
</code></pre>
<h3>모델 설정 해결 순서 <code>configure_model_settings()</code></h3>
<p>3단계로 설정이 결정된다:</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph LR
    A["MODEL_SETTINGS에서&#x3C;br/>정확 이름 매칭"] -->|없으면| B["apply_generic_model_settings()&#x3C;br/>패턴 기반 fallback"]
    A -->|있으면| C["_copy_fields()로&#x3C;br/>전체 필드 복사"]
    B --> D["extra_model_settings&#x3C;br/>deep merge 적용"]
    C --> D
    D --> E["OpenRouter 모델이면&#x3C;br/>thinking_tokens, reasoning_effort 자동 추가"]
    E --> F["최종 Model 인스턴스"]
</code></pre>
<ol>
<li><strong>정확 매칭</strong>: <code>MODEL_SETTINGS</code> 리스트에서 <code>name</code>이 일치하는 <code>ModelSettings</code>를 찾아 필드 복사</li>
<li><strong>패턴 매칭 fallback</strong>: <code>apply_generic_model_settings()</code>에서 문자열 포함 여부로 설정 결정</li>
<li><strong>extra_params 오버레이</strong>: <code>110_aider/extra_params</code> 이름의 특수 ModelSettings가 있으면 deep merge</li>
</ol>
<h3><code>apply_generic_model_settings()</code> — 패턴 매칭 상세</h3>
<p>이 함수가 20+ 패턴 규칙으로 모델 동작을 자동 결정한다. <strong>순서가 중요 — 먼저 매칭되면 <code>return</code>으로 빠져나감</strong>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:421-583 — 주요 패턴 규칙 (실제 소스 코드)
def apply_generic_model_settings(self, model):
    # 1. o3-mini: diff + repo_map + reasoning_effort
    if "/o3-mini" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.use_temperature = False
        self.system_prompt_prefix = "Formatting re-enabled. "
        if "reasoning_effort" not in self.accepts_settings:
            self.accepts_settings.append("reasoning_effort")
        return

    # 2. gpt-4.1-mini: diff + repo_map
    if "gpt-4.1-mini" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.reminder = "sys"
        return

    # 3. gpt-5: diff + reasoning_effort + no temperature
    last_segment = model.split("/")[-1]
    if last_segment in ("gpt-5", "gpt-5-2025-08-07"):
        self.use_temperature = False
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        if "reasoning_effort" not in self.accepts_settings:
            self.accepts_settings.append("reasoning_effort")
        return

    # 4. deepseek v3: diff + repo_map + sys examples
    if "deepseek" in model and "v3" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.reminder = "sys"
        self.examples_as_sys_msg = True
        return

    # 5. deepseek reasoning (r1): diff + reasoning_tag="think"
    if "deepseek" in model and ("r1" in model or "reasoning" in model):
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.use_temperature = False
        self.reasoning_tag = "think"
        return

    # 6. Claude 4.5/4.6: diff + thinking_tokens
    if "sonnet-4-5" in model or "opus-4-6" in model or "haiku-4-5" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.examples_as_sys_msg = False
        if "thinking_tokens" not in self.accepts_settings:
            self.accepts_settings.append("thinking_tokens")
        return

    # 7. qwq-32b: diff + reasoning_tag="think" + temperature=0.6
    if "qwq" in model and "32b" in model and "preview" not in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.reasoning_tag = "think"
        self.use_temperature = 0.6
        self.extra_params = dict(top_p=0.95)
        return

    # 8. qwen3-235b: diff + /no_think prefix + top_k=20
    if "qwen3" in model and "235b" in model:
        self.edit_format = "diff"
        self.use_repo_map = True
        self.system_prompt_prefix = "/no_think"
        self.use_temperature = 0.7
        self.extra_params = {"top_p": 0.8, "top_k": 20, "min_p": 0.0}
        return

    # ... 15+ 추가 규칙 (llama3-70b, gpt-4-turbo, claude-3-opus 등)
</code></pre>
<table>

<tr>

</tr>
</thead>

<h3>ModelInfoManager — 4단계 메타데이터 파이프라인</h3>
<p>모델의 context window, 비용 정보를 4계층으로 관리한다:</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A["get_model_info(model)"] --> B["① local_model_metadata&#x3C;br/>(register_litellm_models)"]
    B -->|"있으면"| Z["반환"]
    B -->|"없으면"| C["② litellm 캐시 DB&#x3C;br/>~/.aider/caches/*.json&#x3C;br/>24h TTL"]
    C -->|"캐시 만료/미존재"| D["GitHub raw URL에서&#x3C;br/>model_prices_and_context_window.json&#x3C;br/>다운로드"]
    D --> C
    C -->|"없으면"| E["③ litellm.get_model_info()&#x3C;br/>(lazy import)"]
    E -->|"없으면 &#x26; openrouter/"| F["④ OpenRouter API 캐시&#x3C;br/>openrouter_manager"]
    F -->|"없으면"| G["⑤ OpenRouter 웹 스크래핑&#x3C;br/>(최후 수단)"]
    G --> Z
    E --> Z
    F --> Z
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:237-262 — 4단계 해석 (실제 소스 코드)
def get_model_info(self, model):
    # ① 사용자 로컬 메타데이터 (최우선)
    cached_info = self.get_model_from_cached_json_db(model)

    # ② litellm 내장 DB (lazy import 최적화)
    litellm_info = None
    if litellm._lazy_module or not cached_info:
        try:
            litellm_info = litellm.get_model_info(model)
        except Exception: pass

    if litellm_info:
        return litellm_info

    # ③ OpenRouter 전용 fallback
    if not cached_info and model.startswith("openrouter/"):
        # 로컬 API 캐시
        openrouter_info = self.openrouter_manager.get_model_info(model)
        if openrouter_info:
            return openrouter_info
        # ④ 웹 스크래핑 (최후 수단)
        openrouter_info = self.fetch_openrouter_model_info(model)
        if openrouter_info:
            return openrouter_info

    return cached_info
</code></pre>
<p><strong>OpenRouter 웹 스크래핑</strong> — litellm DB에도 없는 OpenRouter 모델은 모델 페이지 HTML을 파싱하여 context window와 비용을 추출한다:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:264-308 — 웹 스크래핑 (실제 소스 코드)
def fetch_openrouter_model_info(self, model):
    url_part = model[len("openrouter/"):]
    url = "https://openrouter.ai/" + url_part
    response = requests.get(url, timeout=5)
    html = response.text
    text = re.sub(r"&#x3C;[^>]+>", " ", html)  # HTML 태그 제거
    # 정규식으로 context, input/output 비용 추출
    context_match = re.search(r"([\d,]+)\s*context", text)
    input_cost_match = re.search(r"\$\s*([\d.]+)\s*/M input tokens", text)
    output_cost_match = re.search(r"\$\s*([\d.]+)\s*/M output tokens", text)
    # ...파싱 결과를 dict으로 반환
</code></pre>
<h3>모델 별칭 시스템</h3>
<p><code>MODEL_ALIASES</code> 딕셔너리로 단축 이름을 지원한다:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:87-111 (실제 소스 코드)
MODEL_ALIASES = {
    "sonnet": "claude-sonnet-4-5",
    "haiku": "claude-haiku-4-5",
    "opus": "claude-opus-4-6",
    "4o": "gpt-4o",
    "deepseek": "deepseek/deepseek-chat",
    "flash": "gemini/gemini-flash-latest",
    "flash-lite": "gemini/gemini-2.5-flash-lite",
    "gemini": "gemini/gemini-3-pro-preview",
    "r1": "deepseek/deepseek-reasoner",
    "grok3": "xai/grok-3-beta",
    "optimus": "openrouter/openrouter/optimus-alpha",
    "quasar": "openrouter/openrouter/quasar-alpha",
    # ...
}
</code></pre>
<h3>Fast-Path API 키 검증</h3>
<p><code>fast_validate_environment()</code>가 litellm import 없이 빠르게 키를 검증한다:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 110_aider/models.py:697-726 (실제 소스 코드)
def fast_validate_environment(self):
    """litellm import를 강제하지 않는 빠른 경로"""
    model = self.name
    pieces = model.split("/")
    provider = pieces[0] if len(pieces) > 1 else None

    keymap = dict(
        openrouter="OPENROUTER_API_KEY",
        openai="OPENAI_API_KEY",
        deepseek="DEEPSEEK_API_KEY",
        gemini="GEMINI_API_KEY",
        anthropic="ANTHROPIC_API_KEY",
        groq="GROQ_API_KEY",
        fireworks_ai="FIREWORKS_API_KEY",
    )

    # 하드코딩된 모델 목록으로 provider 매핑
    if model in OPENAI_MODELS:
        var = "OPENAI_API_KEY"
    elif model in ANTHROPIC_MODELS:
        var = "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY"
    else:
        var = keymap.get(provider)

    if var and os.environ.get(var):
        return dict(keys_in_environment=[var], missing_keys=[])
    # None 반환 → 느린 경로(litellm.validate_environment)로 fallback
</code></pre>
<h3>Weak Model / Editor Model 체인</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph LR
    MAIN["주 모델&#x3C;br/>(예: claude-sonnet-4-5)"] --> WEAK["weak_model&#x3C;br/>(커밋 메시지 등)"]
    MAIN --> EDITOR["editor_model&#x3C;br/>(코드 편집 전용)"]
    WEAK --> WMNAME["weak_model_name&#x3C;br/>ModelSettings에서 결정"]
    EDITOR --> EMNAME["editor_model_name&#x3C;br/>ModelSettings에서 결정"]
    EDITOR --> EFMT["editor_edit_format&#x3C;br/>editor-diff / editor-whole"]
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li><strong>Weak model</strong>: 커밋 메시지 생성, 채팅 요약 등 저비용 작업에 사용. 미지정 시 주 모델을 공유.</li>
<li><strong>Editor model</strong>: 코드 편집 전용. <code>editor_edit_format</code>은 자동으로 <code>"editor-"</code> 접두사 추가.</li>
</ul>

<p>Aider is a terminal pair-programming harness. Unlike Codex (<code>co</code>), it does <strong>not</strong> merge remote MCP tool catalogs, spawn stdio/SSE MCP servers, or maintain an <code>mcpServers</code> configuration layer. The corpus audit treats this as <strong>negative evidence</strong>: absence of MCP-shaped modules is itself a design fact worth documenting precisely, because many readers assume every modern agent stack exposes MCP.</p>

# `import litellm` takes 1.5 seconds, defer it!

class LazyLiteLLM:
    _lazy_module = None

    def __getattr__(self, name):
        if name == "_lazy_module":
            return super()
        self._load_litellm()
        return getattr(self._lazy_module, name)

    def _load_litellm(self):
        ...
        self._lazy_module = importlib.import_module("litellm")
        self._lazy_module.suppress_debug_info = True
        self._lazy_module.set_verbose = False
        self._lazy_module.drop_params = True
        self._lazy_module._logging._disable_debugging()

litellm = LazyLiteLLM()
</code></pre>
