<h2>코퍼스 — 009_mcp-orchestration/09_ai_mcp.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Aider MCP Orchestration</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>110_aider/</code> — <strong>no MCP client/server</strong> in the analyzed checkout. Tool orchestration is in-process: LiteLLM for model I/O, <code>Commands</code> for slash extensions, optional Playwright scrape, and linter subprocesses — not Model Context Protocol transports.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Aider is a terminal pair-programming harness. Unlike Codex (<code>co</code>), it does <strong>not</strong> merge remote MCP tool catalogs, spawn stdio/SSE MCP servers, or maintain an <code>mcpServers</code> configuration layer. The corpus audit treats this as <strong>negative evidence</strong>: absence of MCP-shaped modules is itself a design fact worth documenting precisely, because many readers assume every modern agent stack exposes MCP.</p>
<p>This document maps what Aider <em>does</em> use instead — LiteLLM as the unified LLM gateway, slash-command "tools" on <code>Commands</code>, subprocess linters, and optional browser scrape — and contrasts that surface with Codex's <code>McpManager</code> / <code>mcp_tool_call.rs</code> pipeline.</p>
<h2>Executive summary</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Expected MCP role</th>
<th>Aider (<code>110_aider/</code>) status</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>MCP server hosting tools</td>
<td><strong>Absent</strong> — no server module, no tool schema registration</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCP client merging remote tools</td>
<td><strong>Absent</strong> — no stdio/HTTP MCP client</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Config file (<code>mcpServers</code>, <code>mcp.json</code>)</td>
<td><strong>Absent</strong> — <code>.aider.conf.yml</code> / env only</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tool call approval pipeline</td>
<td>Interactive <code>confirm_ask</code> on shell/URL; not MCP annotation-based</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>External process tools</td>
<td>Linter subprocess (<code>linter.py</code>), shell via <code>run_cmd.py</code>, Playwright scrape</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LLM routing</td>
<td><strong>LiteLLM</strong> lazy wrapper (<code>aider/llm.py</code>) — not MCP</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2>Negative evidence audit</h2>
<h3>Repository-wide MCP search</h3>
<p>A full-text search over Python sources under <code>110_aider/aider/</code> for <code>\bmcp\b</code>, <code>Model Context Protocol</code>, and common MCP import paths returns <strong>zero matches</strong> in application code (audited 2026-06-27).</p>
<p>The only incidental hit is a <strong>comment</strong> in the dependency lockfile input:</p>
<pre><code>110_aider/requirements/requirements.in:48
# mcp which is a pywin32 dependency that fails on linux CI.
</code></pre>
<p>That comment refers to an unrelated Windows <code>pywin32</code> transitive dependency — not Aider implementing MCP.</p>
<h3><code>pyproject.toml</code> — no MCP package</h3>
<p><code>110_aider/pyproject.toml:1-49</code> declares the <code>aider-chat</code> package with dynamic dependencies loaded from <code>requirements.txt</code>. Neither file lists an <code>mcp</code> or <code>model-context-protocol</code> Python package. Core runtime deps include <code>litellm==1.82.3</code> (see <code>110_aider/requirements.txt:184</code>) but no MCP SDK.</p>
<h3>CLI entry — no MCP flags</h3>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/main.py:32</code> imports <code>litellm</code> at launch to initialize the lazy module early in some code paths:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">from aider.llm import litellm  # noqa: F401; properly init litellm on launch
</code></pre>
<p><code>main.py:973-1007</code> constructs the session via <code>Coder.create(...)</code> with git, lint, test, and <code>suggest_shell_commands</code> kwargs — <strong>no MCP server list, no tool merge step, no OAuth for MCP transports</strong>.</p>
<h3><code>commands.py</code> — slash surface, not MCP spawn</h3>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/commands.py:36-85</code> defines the <code>Commands</code> class holding <code>io</code>, <code>coder</code>, and CLI <code>args</code>. Command discovery is convention-based (<code>cmd_*</code> methods → <code>/slash</code> names via <code>get_commands()</code> at <code>commands.py:276-285</code>). This is an in-process registry, not dynamic MCP tool listing.</p>
<p>Notable integrations that <em>replace</em> typical MCP tool categories:</p>
<table>

<tr>
<th>User intent</th>

<p>None of these spawn or call MCP servers.</p>
<h2>Architecture — what Aider uses instead of MCP</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A["main.py&#x3C;br/>CLI entry"] --> B["Coder.create()&#x3C;br/>base_coder.py:124-201"]
    B --> C["Coder subclass&#x3C;br/>edit_format plugin"]
    C --> D["litellm.completion&#x3C;br/>models.py / base_coder.py"]
    C --> E["Commands.run()&#x3C;br/>slash commands"]
    E --> F["/web Scraper"]
    E --> G["/run run_cmd.py"]
    E --> H["/lint Linter subprocess"]
    C --> I["run_shell_commands&#x3C;br/>model-suggested shell"]
    I --> G
    D --> J["External LLM APIs&#x3C;br/>via LiteLLM"]
    F --> K["HTTP / Playwright"]
    H --> L["flake8/ruff/etc subprocess"]
    G --> M["Host shell&#x3C;br/>no OS sandbox"]
</code></pre>
<p>The diagram highlights the <strong>single-process</strong> model: the "tool router" is <code>Commands</code> + <code>Coder</code> methods, not a separate MCP connection manager.</p>
<h2>LiteLLM — the actual orchestration hub for models</h2>
<p>Aider defers <code>import litellm</code> because it costs ~1.5s at cold start. The lazy wrapper lives entirely in <code>110_aider/aider/llm.py</code>.</p>
<h3>Lazy module loading</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># llm.py:16-47
# `import litellm` takes 1.5 seconds, defer it!

class LazyLiteLLM:
    _lazy_module = None

    def __getattr__(self, name):
        if name == "_lazy_module":
            return super()
        self._load_litellm()
        return getattr(self._lazy_module, name)

    def _load_litellm(self):
        ...
        self._lazy_module = importlib.import_module("litellm")
        self._lazy_module.suppress_debug_info = True
        self._lazy_module.set_verbose = False
        self._lazy_module.drop_params = True
        self._lazy_module._logging._disable_debugging()

litellm = LazyLiteLLM()
</code></pre>
<p>Environment branding is set before load (<code>llm.py:12-14</code>): <code>OR_SITE_URL</code>, <code>OR_APP_NAME</code>, <code>LITELLM_MODE=PRODUCTION</code>.</p>
<h3>Where LiteLLM is invoked</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>

<th>Citation</th>
</tr>

</tr>

<td><code>base_coder.py</code></td>

</tr>

</tr>

<p><code>110_aider/aider/models.py:1036</code> is the primary chat completion path:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">res = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
</code></pre>
<p>This is the functional equivalent of Codex's model router — but it routes to <strong>LLM providers</strong>, not MCP tool servers. There is no second hop where tool definitions are merged from external MCP processes.</p>
<h3>LiteLLM vs MCP — conceptual boundary</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Layer</th>
<th>Codex (<code>co</code>)</th>
<th>Aider (<code>ai</code>)</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Model API</td>
<td>OpenAI/Codex client + config</td>
<td>LiteLLM unified adapter</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tool definitions</td>
<td>MCP <code>list_tools</code> + built-ins</td>
<td>System prompts + edit formats + slash commands</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tool execution</td>
<td><code>mcp_tool_call.rs</code> pipeline</td>
<td>In-process Python + subprocess</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Config</td>
<td>TOML <code>mcp_servers</code> layers</td>
<td><code>.aider.conf.yml</code>, env vars, CLI flags</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2>Linter subprocess — external tool pattern (not MCP-shaped)</h2>
<p>Aider's closest analogue to "call an external capability" for code quality is the <strong><code>Linter</code></strong> class in <code>110_aider/aider/linter.py</code>. It is <strong>not</strong> MCP: no JSON-RPC, no tool schema, no server lifecycle.</p>
<h3>Construction and wiring</h3>
<p><code>base_coder.py:525-528</code> attaches a linter to every coder session:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">self.linter = Linter(root=self.root, encoding=io.encoding)
self.auto_lint = auto_lint
self.setup_lint_cmds(lint_cmds)
</code></pre>
<p><code>setup_lint_cmds()</code> at <code>base_coder.py:544-548</code> maps language → shell command strings via <code>linter.set_linter(lang, cmd)</code>.</p>
<h3>Subprocess execution path</h3>
<p><code>linter.py:47-68</code> runs configured commands as shell subprocesses:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def run_cmd(self, cmd, rel_fname, code):
    cmd += " " + oslex.quote(rel_fname)
    ...
    returncode, stdout = run_cmd_subprocess(
        cmd,
        cwd=self.root,
        encoding=self.encoding,
    )
</code></pre>
<p>Key properties:</p>
<ul>
<li>Uses <code>run_cmd_subprocess</code> from <code>run_cmd.py</code> (shared with <code>/run</code> and model-suggested shell).</li>
<li>Exit code <code>0</code> means clean; non-zero stdout becomes lint feedback for the model.</li>
<li>Default Python path combines <code>basic_lint</code>, <code>py_lint</code>, and optional tree-sitter context (<code>linter.py:82-116</code>).</li>
</ul>
<h3>Auto-lint in the edit loop</h3>
<p>After applying edits, <code>base_coder.py:1599-1607</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">if edited and self.auto_lint:
    lint_errors = self.lint_edited(edited)
    self.auto_commit(edited, context="Ran the linter")
    ...
    if lint_errors:
        ok = self.io.confirm_ask("Attempt to fix lint errors?")
</code></pre>
<p><code>lint_edited()</code> at <code>base_coder.py:1681-1696</code> calls <code>self.linter.lint()</code> per file. The <code>/lint</code> slash command (<code>commands.py:356-409</code>) can spawn a <strong>clone coder</strong> to fix errors interactively.</p>
<p>This is a <strong>tight coupling</strong> pattern: subprocess output is formatted as chat messages, not normalized MCP <code>CallToolResult</code> content blocks.</p>
<h2>Shell commands — second external integration path</h2>
<p>Model-suggested shell (when <code>suggest_shell_commands=True</code>) follows <code>base_coder.py:2434-2485</code>:</p>
<ol>
<li><code>EditBlockCoder.get_edits()</code> collects shell lines into <code>self.shell_commands</code> (<code>editblock_coder.py:33</code>).</li>
<li><code>run_shell_commands()</code> deduplicates via <code>ConfirmGroup</code>.</li>
<li><code>handle_shell_commands()</code> prompts with <code>explicit_yes_required=True</code>.</li>
<li><code>run_cmd(command, cwd=self.root)</code> executes on the <strong>host</strong> (see sandbox doc <code>07_ai_sandbox.md</code>).</li>
</ol>
<p>This is user-gated execution, not autonomous MCP tool invocation.</p>
<h2>Web scrape — optional Playwright extension</h2>
<p><code>/web</code> at <code>commands.py:219-253</code> lazily constructs a <code>Scraper</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">res = install_playwright(self.io)  # optional extra
self.scraper = Scraper(
    print_error=self.io.tool_error,
    playwright_available=res,
    verify_ssl=self.verify_ssl,
)
content = self.scraper.scrape(url) or ""
</code></pre>
<p>Playwright is an <strong>optional dependency group</strong> (<code>pyproject.toml:35-36</code>: <code>playwright = { file = "requirements/requirements-playwright.txt" }</code>), not an MCP server. JS-heavy pages may need Playwright; static HTML uses simpler fetch paths inside <code>scrape.py</code>.</p>
<h2>URL detection — ConfirmGroup without MCP</h2>
<p>When <code>detect_urls=True</code>, <code>base_coder.py:972</code> uses <code>ConfirmGroup(urls)</code> before fetching links mentioned in chat — same confirmation primitive as shell batches (<code>io.py:82-88</code>). This is orchestration of <strong>network fetch</strong>, not MCP resource templates.</p>
<h2>Integration alternatives (user-operated)</h2>
<p>Because Aider ships no first-party MCP client, users who want MCP-shaped workflows must wrap Aider externally:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Approach</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>MCP host wraps Aider</td>
<td>Run <code>aider</code> as a subprocess tool inside Claude Desktop / Codex / custom MCP server</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Reverse bridge</td>
<td>Expose git/repo tools via MCP separately; developer copies context into Aider manually</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fork extension</td>
<td>Add MCP client to Aider (not present in snapshot)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Use Codex/OmO for MCP</td>
<td>Keep Aider for edit-loop pair programming; use <code>co</code> axis for MCP orchestration</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Related built-in surface (no MCP): <code>003_tool-runtime/03_ai_tool.md</code> if present in corpus.</p>

<h2>Design implications for corpus readers</h2>
<ol>
<li><strong>Do not infer MCP from "agent" label.</strong> Aider is a capable agent loop but uses classic Python extension patterns.</li>
<li><strong>LiteLLM is the integration point</strong> for model providers — document provider keys, model aliases, and <code>models.py</code> when tracing API behavior.</li>
<li><strong>Subprocess tools are ad hoc</strong> — linter commands and <code>/run</code> share <code>run_cmd.py</code> but lack unified schema, timeout policy, or sandbox (contrast Codex <code>tool_timeout_sec</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Negative evidence must be re-audited</strong> on upstream Aider releases; MCP may be added later.</li>
</ol>

3f:Tccc3,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>Aider의 메모리 시스템은 <strong>세션 간 지속 메모리가 없는</strong> 제한적 구조다. <strong>이중 메시지 버퍼(done_messages/cur_messages)</strong> + <strong>ChatSummary 재귀적 head/tail 요약</strong> + <strong>ChatChunks 결정적 프롬프트 조립</strong> + <strong>3종 파일 히스토리(input/chat/llm)</strong> + <strong>Anthropic cache_control 프롬프트 캐싱</strong> + <strong>Coder 포크 시 히스토리 전파</strong> 로 구성된다. Codex의 2-phase extraction/consolidation 파이프라인이나 Copilot CLI의 CompactionProcessor와 달리, 세션 간 학습보다 <strong>단일 세션 내 대화 관리와 토큰 절약</strong>에 집중하는 설계다.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ol>
<li>제한적 범위: Codex vs Copilot CLI vs Aider 비교</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li>이중 메시지 버퍼 — 핵심 상태 관리</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>2.1 버퍼 초기화</li>
<li>2.2 턴 완료 시 병합 (move_back_cur_messages)</li>
<li>2.3 Coder 포크 시 히스토리 전파</li>
<li>
<ol start="3">
<li>ChatSummary — 재귀적 head/tail 요약 엔진</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>3.1 클래스 구조</li>
<li>3.2 max_chat_history_tokens 계산</li>
<li>3.3 too_big 검사</li>
<li>3.4 summarize_real — 재귀적 head/tail 분할 알고리즘</li>
<li>3.5 summarize_all — LLM 요약 실행</li>
<li>3.6 요약 프롬프트</li>
</ul>

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:395-403
if cur_messages:
    self.cur_messages = cur_messages
else:
    self.cur_messages = []

if done_messages:
    self.done_messages = done_messages
else:
    self.done_messages = []
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:1036-1046
def move_back_cur_messages(self, message):
    self.done_messages += self.cur_messages      # 1. cur → done 병합
    self.summarize_start()                        # 2. 요약 필요성 검사 + 시작

    if message:                                    # 3. 최종 상태 메시지 추가
        self.done_messages += [
            dict(role="user", content=message),
            dict(role="assistant", content="Ok."),
        ]
    self.cur_messages = []                         # 4. cur 초기화
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:153-188 — Coder.create() (from_coder 분기)
if from_coder:
    use_kwargs = dict(from_coder.original_kwargs)

    # edit_format이 변경되면 이전 ASSISTANT 메시지가 새 LLM을 혼란시킴
    # → 전체 히스토리를 강제 요약하여 텍스트로 변환
    done_messages = from_coder.done_messages
    if edit_format != from_coder.edit_format and done_messages and summarize_from_coder:
        try:
            done_messages = from_coder.summarizer.summarize_all(done_messages)
        except ValueError:
            io.tool_warning(
                "Chat history summarization failed, continuing with full history"
            )

    update = dict(
        fnames=list(from_coder.abs_fnames),
        read_only_fnames=list(from_coder.abs_read_only_fnames),
        done_messages=done_messages,           # ← 요약된 히스토리 전달
        cur_messages=from_coder.cur_messages,
        aider_commit_hashes=from_coder.aider_commit_hashes,
        total_cost=from_coder.total_cost,
        total_tokens_sent=from_coder.total_tokens_sent,
        total_tokens_received=from_coder.total_tokens_received,
        # ...
    )
</code></pre>

        self.token_count = self.models[0].token_count

<pre><code class="language-python"># history.py:15-18
def too_big(self, messages):
    sized = self.tokenize(messages)
    total = sum(tokens for tokens, _msg in sized)
    return total > self.max_tokens
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A["summarize_real(messages, depth)"] --> B{"total ≤ max_tokens AND depth==0?"}
    B -->|Yes| C["그대로 반환"]
    B -->|No| D{"len ≤ 4 OR depth > 3?"}
    D -->|Yes| E["summarize_all(messages)"]
    D -->|No| F["역순 순회: tail에 max_tokens/2 할당"]
    F --> G["split_index 결정&#x3C;br/>(assistant 메시지 경계 조정)"]
    G --> H{"split_index ≤ 4?"}
    H -->|Yes| E
    H -->|No| I["head 자르기 (모델 입력 한도 - 512)"]
    I --> J["summarize_all(head)"]
    J --> K{"summary + tail ≤ max_tokens?"}
    K -->|Yes| L["summary + tail 반환"]
    K -->|No| M["summarize_real(summary+tail, depth+1)"]
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># history.py:33-96 — 전체 알고리즘
def summarize_real(self, messages, depth=0):
    sized = self.tokenize(messages)
    total = sum(tokens for tokens, _msg in sized)

    # 1. 전체가 한도 이내이면 그대로 반환 (depth==0에서만)
    if total &#x3C;= self.max_tokens and depth == 0:
        return messages

    # 2. 메시지 4개 이하 또는 재귀 깊이 3 초과 → 전체 요약
    min_split = 4
    if len(messages) &#x3C;= min_split or depth > 3:
        return self.summarize_all(messages)

    # 3. tail: max_tokens/2 이내의 최신 메시지를 역순으로 보존
    tail_tokens = 0
    split_index = len(messages)
    half_max_tokens = self.max_tokens // 2

    for i in range(len(sized) - 1, -1, -1):
        tokens, _msg = sized[i]
        if tail_tokens + tokens &#x3C; half_max_tokens:
            tail_tokens += tokens
            split_index = i
        else:
            break

    # 4. head가 assistant 메시지로 끝나도록 경계 조정
    while messages[split_index - 1]["role"] != "assistant" and split_index > 1:
        split_index -= 1

    if split_index &#x3C;= min_split:
        return self.summarize_all(messages)

    tail = messages[split_index:]

    # 5. head를 모델 입력 한도 내로 자르기
    model_max_input_tokens = self.models[0].info.get("max_input_tokens") or 4096
    model_max_input_tokens -= 512  # 안전 버퍼

    keep = []
    total = 0
    for tokens, msg in sized[:split_index]:
        total += tokens
        if total > model_max_input_tokens:
            break
        keep.append(msg)

    # 6. head 요약
    summary = self.summarize_all(keep)

    # 7. 요약 + tail이 한도 이내면 반환, 아니면 재귀
    summary_tokens = self.token_count(summary)
    tail_tokens = sum(tokens for tokens, _ in sized[split_index:])
    if summary_tokens + tail_tokens &#x3C; self.max_tokens:
        return summary + tail

    return self.summarize_real(summary + tail, depth + 1)
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># history.py:98-123
def summarize_all(self, messages):
    content = ""
    for msg in messages:
        role = msg["role"].upper()
        if role not in ("USER", "ASSISTANT"):
            continue
        content += f"# {role}\n"
        content += msg["content"]
        if not content.endswith("\n"):
            content += "\n"

    summarize_messages = [
        dict(role="system", content=prompts.summarize),
        dict(role="user", content=content),
    ]

    for model in self.models:                     # weak_model 먼저 시도
        try:
            summary = model.simple_send_with_retries(summarize_messages)
            if summary is not None:
                summary = prompts.summary_prefix + summary
                return [dict(role="user", content=summary)]  # ← user 역할로 주입
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Summarization failed for model {model.name}: {str(e)}")

    raise ValueError("summarizer unexpectedly failed for all models")
</code></pre>

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:1002-1034

# 1. summarize_start: 필요성 검사 + 스레드 시작
def summarize_start(self):
    if not self.summarizer.too_big(self.done_messages):
        return
    self.summarize_end()                 # 이전 요약 완료 대기
    self.summarizer_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.summarize_worker)
    self.summarizer_thread.start()

# 2. summarize_worker: 백그라운드에서 요약 실행
def summarize_worker(self):
    self.summarizing_messages = list(self.done_messages)    # 스냅샷
    try:
        self.summarized_done_messages = self.summarizer.summarize(self.summarizing_messages)
    except ValueError as err:
        self.io.tool_warning(err.args[0])

# 3. summarize_end: 결과 수거 + done_messages 교체
def summarize_end(self):
    if self.summarizer_thread is None:
        return
    self.summarizer_thread.join()
    self.summarizer_thread = None

    # optimistic concurrency: 스냅샷과 현재가 같을 때만 교체
    if self.summarizing_messages == self.done_messages:
        self.done_messages = self.summarized_done_messages
    self.summarizing_messages = None
    self.summarized_done_messages = []
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/chat_chunks.py:5-26
@dataclass
class ChatChunks:
    system: List       # 시스템 프롬프트
    examples: List     # few-shot 예시
    readonly_files: List  # 읽기 전용 파일
    repo: List         # repo-map
    done: List         # ← 요약된 이전 대화 (done_messages)
    chat_files: List   # 편집 대상 파일
    cur: List          # ← 현재 턴 (cur_messages)
    reminder: List     # 리마인더 프롬프트

    def all_messages(self):
        return (
            self.system
            + self.examples
            + self.readonly_files
            + self.repo
            + self.done          # 5번째 위치
            + self.chat_files    # 6번째 위치
            + self.cur           # 7번째 위치
            + self.reminder      # 8번째 (마지막)
        )
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/chat_chunks.py:28-55
def add_cache_control_headers(self):
    # 1순위: examples (없으면 system)
    if self.examples:
        self.add_cache_control(self.examples)
    else:
        self.add_cache_control(self.system)

    # 2순위: repo (없으면 readonly_files)
    if self.repo:
        self.add_cache_control(self.repo)
    else:
        self.add_cache_control(self.readonly_files)

    # 3순위: chat_files (항상)
    self.add_cache_control(self.chat_files)

def add_cache_control(self, messages):
    if not messages:
        return
    content = messages[-1]["content"]
    if type(content) is str:
        content = dict(type="text", text=content)
    content["cache_control"] = {"type": "ephemeral"}
    messages[-1]["content"] = [content]
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/chat_chunks.py:57-64
def cacheable_messages(self):
    messages = self.all_messages()
    for i, message in enumerate(reversed(messages)):
        if isinstance(message.get("content"), list) and message["content"][0].get(
            "cache_control"
        ):
            return messages[: len(messages) - i]
    return messages
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:1340-1394
def warm_cache(self, chunks):
    if not self.add_cache_headers:
        return
    if not self.num_cache_warming_pings:
        return

    delay = 5 * 60 - 5                              # 4분 55초 (5분 TTL 직전)
    delay = float(os.environ.get("AIDER_CACHE_KEEPALIVE_DELAY", delay))
    self.next_cache_warm = time.time() + delay
    self.warming_pings_left = self.num_cache_warming_pings
    self.cache_warming_chunks = chunks

    def warm_cache_worker():
        while self.ok_to_warm_cache:
            time.sleep(1)
            if self.warming_pings_left &#x3C;= 0:
                continue
            now = time.time()
            if now &#x3C; self.next_cache_warm:
                continue

            self.warming_pings_left -= 1
            self.next_cache_warm = time.time() + delay

            kwargs = dict(self.main_model.extra_params) or dict()
            kwargs["max_tokens"] = 1                 # 최소 토큰으로 비용 최소화

            completion = litellm.completion(
                model=self.main_model.name,
                messages=self.cache_warming_chunks.cacheable_messages(),
                stream=False,
                **kwargs,
            )

            cache_hit_tokens = getattr(
                completion.usage, "prompt_cache_hit_tokens", 0
            ) or getattr(completion.usage, "cache_read_input_tokens", 0)

    self.cache_warming_thread = threading.Timer(0, warm_cache_worker)
    self.cache_warming_thread.daemon = True
    self.cache_warming_thread.start()
</code></pre>

<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># utils.py:148-196 — 마크다운→메시지 변환기
def split_chat_history_markdown(text, include_tool=False):
    messages = []
    user = []
    assistant = []
    tool = []
    lines = text.splitlines(keepends=True)

    for line in lines:
        if line.startswith("# "):          # H1 제목 → 무시
            continue
        if line.startswith("> "):          # blockquote → tool 메시지
            # assistant 먼저 flush, user flush, tool에 추가
            tool.append(line[2:])
            continue
        if line.startswith("#### "):       # H4 → user 메시지
            # assistant flush, tool flush, user에 추가
            content = line[5:]
            user.append(content)
            continue
        # 그 외 → assistant 메시지
        assistant.append(line)

    if not include_tool:
        messages = [m for m in messages if m["role"] != "tool"]
    return messages
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>

def log_llm_history(self, role, content):
    timestamp = datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="seconds")
    with open(self.llm_history_file, "a", encoding="utf-8") as log_file:
        log_file.write(f"{role.upper()} {timestamp}\n")
        log_file.write(content + "\n")

<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:1396-1417
def check_tokens(self, messages):
    input_tokens = self.main_model.token_count(messages)
    max_input_tokens = self.main_model.info.get("max_input_tokens") or 0

    if max_input_tokens and input_tokens >= max_input_tokens:
        self.io.tool_error(
            f"Your estimated chat context of {input_tokens:,} tokens exceeds the"
            f" {max_input_tokens:,} token limit for {self.main_model.name}!"
        )
        self.io.tool_output("To reduce the chat context:")
        self.io.tool_output("- Use /drop to remove unneeded files from the chat")
        self.io.tool_output("- Use /clear to clear the chat history")
        self.io.tool_output("- Break your code into smaller files")

        if not self.io.confirm_ask("Try to proceed anyway?"):
            return False
    return True
</code></pre>

<h2>코퍼스 — 010_memory-pipeline/10_ai_memory.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Aider 메모리·히스토리 파이프라인 분석</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>110_aider/</code> — memory pipeline.</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>⚠️ <strong>소스 기반 분석</strong>: <code>110_aider/history.py</code>의 ChatSummary (144줄), <code>coders/base_coder.py</code>의 이중 버퍼·요약 오케스트레이션·캐시 워밍·Coder 포크 (2486줄), <code>coders/chat_chunks.py</code>의 ChatChunks 메시지 조립 (65줄), <code>utils.py</code>의 split_chat_history_markdown 파서, <code>models.py</code>의 max_chat_history_tokens 계산에 기반한다.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Aider의 메모리 시스템은 <strong>세션 간 지속 메모리가 없는</strong> 제한적 구조다. <strong>이중 메시지 버퍼(done_messages/cur_messages)</strong> + <strong>ChatSummary 재귀적 head/tail 요약</strong> + <strong>ChatChunks 결정적 프롬프트 조립</strong> + <strong>3종 파일 히스토리(input/chat/llm)</strong> + <strong>Anthropic cache_control 프롬프트 캐싱</strong> + <strong>Coder 포크 시 히스토리 전파</strong> 로 구성된다. Codex의 2-phase extraction/consolidation 파이프라인이나 Copilot CLI의 CompactionProcessor와 달리, 세션 간 학습보다 <strong>단일 세션 내 대화 관리와 토큰 절약</strong>에 집중하는 설계다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A["사용자 입력"] --> B["cur_messages 축적"]
    B --> C["LLM 호출 &#x26; 응답"]
    C --> D["move_back_cur_messages()"]
    D --> E["done_messages에 병합"]
    E --> F{"too_big?"}
    F -->|Yes| G["summarize_start() — 백그라운드 스레드"]
    G --> H["ChatSummary.summarize_real()"]
    H --> I["done_messages 교체"]
    F -->|No| J["유지"]

    subgraph "파일 히스토리 (세션 간 유일한 지속)"
        K["input_history_file — prompt_toolkit FileHistory"]
        L["chat_history_file — Markdown append-only"]
        M["llm_history_file — role+timestamp 로그"]
    end

    subgraph "캐시 시스템"
        N["add_cache_control_headers() — Anthropic cache_control"]
        O["warm_cache_worker() — 5분 간격 keepalive"]
    end

    A --> K
    A --> L
    C --> L
    C --> M
</code></pre>

<h2>2. 이중 메시지 버퍼 — 핵심 상태 관리</h2>
<h3>2.1 버퍼 초기화</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:395-403
if cur_messages:
    self.cur_messages = cur_messages
else:
    self.cur_messages = []

if done_messages:
    self.done_messages = done_messages
else:
    self.done_messages = []
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li><strong><code>cur_messages</code></strong>: 현재 턴의 user/assistant 교환. LLM 호출이 완료되면 <code>done_messages</code>로 이동</li>
<li><strong><code>done_messages</code></strong>: 이전 턴들의 누적. 토큰 한도 초과 시 요약 대상</li>
</ul>
<h3>2.2 턴 완료 시 병합 (move_back_cur_messages)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:1036-1046
def move_back_cur_messages(self, message):
    self.done_messages += self.cur_messages      # 1. cur → done 병합
    self.summarize_start()                        # 2. 요약 필요성 검사 + 시작

    if message:                                    # 3. 최종 상태 메시지 추가
        self.done_messages += [
            dict(role="user", content=message),
            dict(role="assistant", content="Ok."),
        ]
    self.cur_messages = []                         # 4. cur 초기화
</code></pre>
<p><strong>핵심 포인트</strong>: <code>message</code> 파라미터는 에디트 결과 요약이나 에러 메시지로, <code>user→assistant("Ok.")</code> 쌍으로 추가된다. 이 패턴은 LLM이 이전 결과를 "인지"하는 것처럼 동작하게 한다.</p>
<h3>2.3 Coder 포크 시 히스토리 전파</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:153-188 — Coder.create() (from_coder 분기)
if from_coder:
    use_kwargs = dict(from_coder.original_kwargs)

    # edit_format이 변경되면 이전 ASSISTANT 메시지가 새 LLM을 혼란시킴
    # → 전체 히스토리를 강제 요약하여 텍스트로 변환
    done_messages = from_coder.done_messages
    if edit_format != from_coder.edit_format and done_messages and summarize_from_coder:
        try:
            done_messages = from_coder.summarizer.summarize_all(done_messages)
        except ValueError:
            io.tool_warning(
                "Chat history summarization failed, continuing with full history"
            )

    update = dict(
        fnames=list(from_coder.abs_fnames),
        read_only_fnames=list(from_coder.abs_read_only_fnames),
        done_messages=done_messages,           # ← 요약된 히스토리 전달
        cur_messages=from_coder.cur_messages,
        aider_commit_hashes=from_coder.aider_commit_hashes,
        total_cost=from_coder.total_cost,
        total_tokens_sent=from_coder.total_tokens_sent,
        total_tokens_received=from_coder.total_tokens_received,
        # ...
    )
</code></pre>
<p><strong>핵심 포인트</strong>: Architect → Editor 전환 등 edit_format이 바뀔 때, 이전 diff/whole 형식의 ASSISTANT 메시지가 새 LLM을 혼란시키므로 <code>summarize_all()</code>로 강제 요약한다. 실패 시 원본 히스토리를 유지하고 경고만 출력한다.</p>

<h3>3.3 too_big 검사</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># history.py:15-18
def too_big(self, messages):
    sized = self.tokenize(messages)
    total = sum(tokens for tokens, _msg in sized)
    return total > self.max_tokens
</code></pre>
<h3>3.4 summarize_real — 재귀적 head/tail 분할 알고리즘</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A["summarize_real(messages, depth)"] --> B{"total ≤ max_tokens AND depth==0?"}
    B -->|Yes| C["그대로 반환"]
    B -->|No| D{"len ≤ 4 OR depth > 3?"}
    D -->|Yes| E["summarize_all(messages)"]
    D -->|No| F["역순 순회: tail에 max_tokens/2 할당"]
    F --> G["split_index 결정&#x3C;br/>(assistant 메시지 경계 조정)"]
    G --> H{"split_index ≤ 4?"}
    H -->|Yes| E
    H -->|No| I["head 자르기 (모델 입력 한도 - 512)"]
    I --> J["summarize_all(head)"]
    J --> K{"summary + tail ≤ max_tokens?"}
    K -->|Yes| L["summary + tail 반환"]
    K -->|No| M["summarize_real(summary+tail, depth+1)"]
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="language-python"># history.py:33-96 — 전체 알고리즘
def summarize_real(self, messages, depth=0):
    sized = self.tokenize(messages)
    total = sum(tokens for tokens, _msg in sized)

    # 1. 전체가 한도 이내이면 그대로 반환 (depth==0에서만)
    if total &#x3C;= self.max_tokens and depth == 0:
        return messages

    # 2. 메시지 4개 이하 또는 재귀 깊이 3 초과 → 전체 요약
    min_split = 4
    if len(messages) &#x3C;= min_split or depth > 3:
        return self.summarize_all(messages)

    # 3. tail: max_tokens/2 이내의 최신 메시지를 역순으로 보존
    tail_tokens = 0
    split_index = len(messages)
    half_max_tokens = self.max_tokens // 2

    for i in range(len(sized) - 1, -1, -1):
        tokens, _msg = sized[i]
        if tail_tokens + tokens &#x3C; half_max_tokens:
            tail_tokens += tokens
            split_index = i
        else:
            break

    # 4. head가 assistant 메시지로 끝나도록 경계 조정
    while messages[split_index - 1]["role"] != "assistant" and split_index > 1:
        split_index -= 1

    if split_index &#x3C;= min_split:
        return self.summarize_all(messages)

    tail = messages[split_index:]

    # 5. head를 모델 입력 한도 내로 자르기
    model_max_input_tokens = self.models[0].info.get("max_input_tokens") or 4096
    model_max_input_tokens -= 512  # 안전 버퍼

    keep = []
    total = 0
    for tokens, msg in sized[:split_index]:
        total += tokens
        if total > model_max_input_tokens:
            break
        keep.append(msg)

    # 6. head 요약
    summary = self.summarize_all(keep)

    # 7. 요약 + tail이 한도 이내면 반환, 아니면 재귀
    summary_tokens = self.token_count(summary)
    tail_tokens = sum(tokens for tokens, _ in sized[split_index:])
    if summary_tokens + tail_tokens &#x3C; self.max_tokens:
        return summary + tail

    return self.summarize_real(summary + tail, depth + 1)
</code></pre>
<p><strong>핵심 설계 결정</strong>:</p>
<ol>
<li>tail(최신 메시지)을 <strong>원본 그대로</strong> 보존 — 최근 컨텍스트의 정확도 우선</li>
<li>head(오래된 메시지)만 요약 — 정보 손실을 과거에 집중</li>
<li>assistant 메시지 경계에서 분할 — 불완전한 user/assistant 쌍 방지</li>
<li>모델 입력 한도 - 512 버퍼 — 요약 프롬프트 자체의 오버헤드 고려</li>
</ol>
<h3>3.5 summarize_all — LLM 요약 실행</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># history.py:98-123
def summarize_all(self, messages):
    content = ""
    for msg in messages:
        role = msg["role"].upper()
        if role not in ("USER", "ASSISTANT"):
            continue
        content += f"# {role}\n"
        content += msg["content"]
        if not content.endswith("\n"):
            content += "\n"

    summarize_messages = [
        dict(role="system", content=prompts.summarize),
        dict(role="user", content=content),
    ]

    for model in self.models:                     # weak_model 먼저 시도
        try:
            summary = model.simple_send_with_retries(summarize_messages)
            if summary is not None:
                summary = prompts.summary_prefix + summary
                return [dict(role="user", content=summary)]  # ← user 역할로 주입
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Summarization failed for model {model.name}: {str(e)}")

    raise ValueError("summarizer unexpectedly failed for all models")
</code></pre>
<p><strong>핵심 포인트</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>system</code> 역할이 아닌 메시지만 요약 대상 (<code>USER</code>, <code>ASSISTANT</code>만)</li>
<li>요약 결과는 <code>user</code> 역할 메시지로 주입 → LLM 관점에서 사용자가 이전 대화를 상기시키는 형태</li>
<li><code>models</code> 배열에서 <strong>weak_model을 먼저</strong> 시도 → 비용 절감</li>
</ul>
<h3>3.6 요약 프롬프트</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># prompts.py:46-58
summarize = """*Briefly* summarize this partial conversation about programming.
Include less detail about older parts and more detail about the most recent messages.
Start a new paragraph every time the topic changes!
...
Phrase the summary with the USER in first person, telling the ASSISTANT about the conversation.
Write *as* the user.
Start the summary with "I asked you..."."""

summary_prefix = "I spoke to you previously about a number of things.\n"
</code></pre>

<h2>4. 비동기 요약 오케스트레이션</h2>
<h3>4.1 summarizer 초기화</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:510-517
self.summarizer = summarizer or ChatSummary(
    [self.main_model.weak_model, self.main_model],  # weak 우선, main fallback
    self.main_model.max_chat_history_tokens,
)

self.summarizer_thread = None
self.summarized_done_messages = []
self.summarizing_messages = None
</code></pre>
<h3>4.2 3단계 비동기 실행</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:1002-1034

# 1. summarize_start: 필요성 검사 + 스레드 시작
def summarize_start(self):
    if not self.summarizer.too_big(self.done_messages):
        return
    self.summarize_end()                 # 이전 요약 완료 대기
    self.summarizer_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.summarize_worker)
    self.summarizer_thread.start()

# 2. summarize_worker: 백그라운드에서 요약 실행
def summarize_worker(self):
    self.summarizing_messages = list(self.done_messages)    # 스냅샷
    try:
        self.summarized_done_messages = self.summarizer.summarize(self.summarizing_messages)
    except ValueError as err:
        self.io.tool_warning(err.args[0])

# 3. summarize_end: 결과 수거 + done_messages 교체
def summarize_end(self):
    if self.summarizer_thread is None:
        return
    self.summarizer_thread.join()
    self.summarizer_thread = None

    # optimistic concurrency: 스냅샷과 현재가 같을 때만 교체
    if self.summarizing_messages == self.done_messages:
        self.done_messages = self.summarized_done_messages
    self.summarizing_messages = None
    self.summarized_done_messages = []
</code></pre>
<p><strong>핵심 포인트</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>summarize_end()</code>에서 <strong>동등성 검사</strong>(<code>self.summarizing_messages == self.done_messages</code>)로 경쟁 조건 방지 — 요약 중 새 메시지가 추가됐다면 요약 결과를 버린다</li>
<li>사용자 입력 대기 동안 백그라운드에서 요약이 진행되므로 UX에 영향 없음</li>
<li>에러 시 <code>ValueError</code> 경고만 출력하고 <code>done_messages</code>는 변경하지 않음</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>5. 프롬프트 조립: ChatChunks</h2>
<h3>5.1 결정적 메시지 순서</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/chat_chunks.py:5-26
@dataclass
class ChatChunks:
    system: List       # 시스템 프롬프트
    examples: List     # few-shot 예시
    readonly_files: List  # 읽기 전용 파일
    repo: List         # repo-map
    done: List         # ← 요약된 이전 대화 (done_messages)
    chat_files: List   # 편집 대상 파일
    cur: List          # ← 현재 턴 (cur_messages)
    reminder: List     # 리마인더 프롬프트

    def all_messages(self):
        return (
            self.system
            + self.examples
            + self.readonly_files
            + self.repo
            + self.done          # 5번째 위치
            + self.chat_files    # 6번째 위치
            + self.cur           # 7번째 위치
            + self.reminder      # 8번째 (마지막)
        )
</code></pre>
<p><strong>위치 의미</strong>: <code>done</code>이 <code>chat_files</code>보다 앞에 위치하므로, LLM 관점에서 파일 컨텍스트(chat_files)가 요약된 히스토리(done)보다 <strong>뒤에 와서 더 중요</strong>하게 취급된다. <code>reminder</code>가 맨 뒤에서 최종 지시를 강화한다.</p>
<h3>5.2 Anthropic cache_control 헤더</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/chat_chunks.py:28-55
def add_cache_control_headers(self):
    # 1순위: examples (없으면 system)
    if self.examples:
        self.add_cache_control(self.examples)
    else:
        self.add_cache_control(self.system)

    # 2순위: repo (없으면 readonly_files)
    if self.repo:
        self.add_cache_control(self.repo)
    else:
        self.add_cache_control(self.readonly_files)

    # 3순위: chat_files (항상)
    self.add_cache_control(self.chat_files)

def add_cache_control(self, messages):
    if not messages:
        return
    content = messages[-1]["content"]
    if type(content) is str:
        content = dict(type="text", text=content)
    content["cache_control"] = {"type": "ephemeral"}
    messages[-1]["content"] = [content]
</code></pre>
<p><strong>핵심 포인트</strong>: <code>done</code>(히스토리)과 <code>cur</code>(현재 턴)에는 캐시 태그를 부여하지 <strong>않는다</strong> — 매 턴마다 변경되므로 캐시 효율이 낮기 때문이다. 불변 콘텐츠(<code>system</code>, <code>examples</code>, <code>repo</code>, <code>chat_files</code>)만 캐시한다.</p>
<h3>5.3 cacheable_messages — 캐시 경계 추출</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/chat_chunks.py:57-64
def cacheable_messages(self):
    messages = self.all_messages()
    for i, message in enumerate(reversed(messages)):
        if isinstance(message.get("content"), list) and message["content"][0].get(
            "cache_control"
        ):
            return messages[: len(messages) - i]
    return messages
</code></pre>
<p>캐시 가능한 메시지만 추출하여 cache warming에 사용한다.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Cache Warming — 프롬프트 캐시 유지</h2>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:1340-1394
def warm_cache(self, chunks):
    if not self.add_cache_headers:
        return
    if not self.num_cache_warming_pings:
        return

    delay = 5 * 60 - 5                              # 4분 55초 (5분 TTL 직전)
    delay = float(os.environ.get("AIDER_CACHE_KEEPALIVE_DELAY", delay))
    self.next_cache_warm = time.time() + delay
    self.warming_pings_left = self.num_cache_warming_pings
    self.cache_warming_chunks = chunks

    def warm_cache_worker():
        while self.ok_to_warm_cache:
            time.sleep(1)
            if self.warming_pings_left &#x3C;= 0:
                continue
            now = time.time()
            if now &#x3C; self.next_cache_warm:
                continue

            self.warming_pings_left -= 1
            self.next_cache_warm = time.time() + delay

            kwargs = dict(self.main_model.extra_params) or dict()
            kwargs["max_tokens"] = 1                 # 최소 토큰으로 비용 최소화

            completion = litellm.completion(
                model=self.main_model.name,
                messages=self.cache_warming_chunks.cacheable_messages(),
                stream=False,
                **kwargs,
            )

            cache_hit_tokens = getattr(
                completion.usage, "prompt_cache_hit_tokens", 0
            ) or getattr(completion.usage, "cache_read_input_tokens", 0)

    self.cache_warming_thread = threading.Timer(0, warm_cache_worker)
    self.cache_warming_thread.daemon = True
    self.cache_warming_thread.start()
</code></pre>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>파라미터</th>
<th>기본값</th>
<th>환경변수</th>
<th>설명</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>delay</code></td>
<td>295초 (4분55초)</td>
<td><code>AIDER_CACHE_KEEPALIVE_DELAY</code></td>
<td>캐시 갱신 간격</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>num_cache_warming_pings</code></td>
<td>0 (비활성)</td>
<td><code>--cache-warming-pings</code></td>
<td>핑 횟수</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>max_tokens</code></td>
<td>1</td>
<td>—</td>
<td>비용 최소화</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h2>7. 세 가지 파일 히스토리</h2>
<h3>7.1 입력 히스토리 (<code>input_history_file</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># io.py:736-752
def add_to_input_history(self, inp):
    FileHistory(self.input_history_file).append_string(inp)

def get_input_history(self):
    fh = FileHistory(self.input_history_file)
    return fh.load_history_strings()
</code></pre>
<p><code>prompt_toolkit.FileHistory</code> 기반. 쉘의 <code>.bash_history</code>와 동일한 역할로, 화살표 키로 이전 입력을 탐색할 수 있다. <strong>LLM에는 전달되지 않는다.</strong></p>
<h3>7.2 채팅 히스토리 (<code>chat_history_file</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># io.py:1117-1136
def append_chat_history(self, text, linebreak=False, blockquote=False, strip=True):
    if blockquote:
        text = "> " + text
    # chat_history_file에 append
</code></pre>
<p>Markdown 형식의 append-only 로그. <code>--restore-chat-history</code> 옵션 사용 시 <strong>유일한 세션 간 대화 복원 경로</strong>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:519-523
if not self.done_messages and restore_chat_history:
    history_md = self.io.read_text(self.io.chat_history_file)
    if history_md:
        self.done_messages = utils.split_chat_history_markdown(history_md)
        self.summarize_start()   # 즉시 요약 시작 (큰 히스토리 대비)
</code></pre>
<h3>7.3 split_chat_history_markdown — Markdown 파서</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># utils.py:148-196 — 마크다운→메시지 변환기
def split_chat_history_markdown(text, include_tool=False):
    messages = []
    user = []
    assistant = []
    tool = []
    lines = text.splitlines(keepends=True)

    for line in lines:
        if line.startswith("# "):          # H1 제목 → 무시
            continue
        if line.startswith("> "):          # blockquote → tool 메시지
            # assistant 먼저 flush, user flush, tool에 추가
            tool.append(line[2:])
            continue
        if line.startswith("#### "):       # H4 → user 메시지
            # assistant flush, tool flush, user에 추가
            content = line[5:]
            user.append(content)
            continue
        # 그 외 → assistant 메시지
        assistant.append(line)

    if not include_tool:
        messages = [m for m in messages if m["role"] != "tool"]
    return messages
</code></pre>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Markdown 패턴</th>
<th>역할 매핑</th>
<th>설명</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code># ...</code></td>
<td>(무시)</td>
<td>세션 제목</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>#### ...</code></td>
<td><code>user</code></td>
<td>사용자 입력</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>> ...</code></td>
<td><code>tool</code></td>
<td>도구 출력</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>일반 텍스트</td>
<td><code>assistant</code></td>
<td>LLM 응답</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>7.4 LLM 히스토리 (<code>llm_history_file</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># io.py:754-765
def log_llm_history(self, role, content):
    timestamp = datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="seconds")
    with open(self.llm_history_file, "a", encoding="utf-8") as log_file:
        log_file.write(f"{role.upper()} {timestamp}\n")
        log_file.write(content + "\n")
</code></pre>
<p>디버깅/감사용 플랫 텍스트 로그. LLM 피드백 루프에 재진입하지 않는다.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. 토큰 한도 검사 (check_tokens)</h2>
<pre><code class="language-python"># coders/base_coder.py:1396-1417
def check_tokens(self, messages):
    input_tokens = self.main_model.token_count(messages)
    max_input_tokens = self.main_model.info.get("max_input_tokens") or 0

    if max_input_tokens and input_tokens >= max_input_tokens:
        self.io.tool_error(
            f"Your estimated chat context of {input_tokens:,} tokens exceeds the"
            f" {max_input_tokens:,} token limit for {self.main_model.name}!"
        )
        self.io.tool_output("To reduce the chat context:")
        self.io.tool_output("- Use /drop to remove unneeded files from the chat")
        self.io.tool_output("- Use /clear to clear the chat history")
        self.io.tool_output("- Break your code into smaller files")

        if not self.io.confirm_ask("Try to proceed anyway?"):
            return False
    return True
</code></pre>
<p><strong>핵심 포인트</strong>: Copilot CLI의 BasicTruncator와 달리, Aider는 한도 초과 시 자동 트렁케이션 없이 <strong>사용자에게 확인</strong>을 요청한다. 자동 압축은 <code>ChatSummary</code>의 <code>too_big()</code> 트리거에 의존한다.</p>
<hr>

<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>Executive summary</li>
<li>Negative evidence — no plugin manifest</li>
<li>Architecture</li>
<li><code>Commands</code> class — slash-command registry</li>
<li>Construction and cloning</li>
<li>Convention-based registration</li>
<li>Dispatch pipeline</li>
<li><code>SwitchCoder</code> — runtime mode switch without plugins</li>
<li><code>/chat-mode</code> — enumerates coder registry</li>
<li>Help command spawns another coder</li>

<li>Classmethod signature and selection loop</li>

def get_commands(self):
    commands = []
    for attr in dir(self):
        if not attr.startswith("cmd_"):
            continue
        cmd = attr[4:]
        cmd = cmd.replace("_", "-")
        commands.append("/" + cmd)
    return commands

<h2>코퍼스 — 011_plugin-system/11_ai_plugin.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Aider Plugin System</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>110_aider/</code> — extension via in-tree <strong><code>Commands</code></strong> slash handlers and <strong><code>Coder.create</code></strong> edit-format factory; <strong>no <code>plugin.json</code></strong>, marketplace, or dynamic plugin loader.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Aider's "plugin system" is really two cooperating registries inside the Python package:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong><code>Commands</code></strong> — user-facing <code>/slash</code> commands discovered by naming convention (<code>cmd_*</code> methods).</li>
<li><strong><code>aider.coders</code></strong> — edit-format "plugins" (subclasses of <code>Coder</code>) selected by <code>Coder.create(edit_format=...)</code>.</li>
</ol>
<p>There is no third-party plugin ABI comparable to Codex's <code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json</code>, Claude Code hooks, or SKILL.md packs. Extending Aider for end users means editing source, maintaining a fork, or wrapping the CLI externally.</p>
<h2>Executive summary</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Extension surface</th>
<th>Mechanism</th>
<th>Dynamic load?</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Slash commands</td>
<td><code>Commands.cmd_*</code> → <code>/name</code></td>
<td>No — static class methods</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Edit formats</td>
<td><code>Coder</code> subclasses in <code>coders/__init__.py</code></td>
<td>No — import-time registry</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chat modes</td>
<td><code>/chat-mode</code>, <code>/architect</code>, etc. → <code>SwitchCoder</code></td>
<td>Switches coder class at runtime</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Config</td>
<td><code>.aider.conf.yml</code>, env, CLI (<code>args.py</code>)</td>
<td>Not plugin bundles</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>GUI</td>
<td><code>aider/gui.py</code> Streamlit front-end</td>
<td>Separate entry, same coders</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCP / hooks</td>
<td>N/A</td>
<td>Absent</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2>Negative evidence — no plugin manifest</h2>
<p>Corpus audit for <code>plugin.json</code>, <code>.codex-plugin</code>, dynamic <code>importlib</code> plugin discovery, or marketplace install under <code>110_aider/aider/</code> returns <strong>no application-level plugin loader</strong>.</p>
<p>Grep for <code>plugin.json</code> in <code>110_aider/</code> hits only unrelated strings (pytest <code>plugins:</code> headers in test fixtures, NeoVim plugin docs in <code>HISTORY.md</code>). <strong>No manifest file format exists in core.</strong></p>
<p>Dependencies in <code>110_aider/pyproject.toml:1-49</code> declare a single package <code>aider</code> with scripts entry <code>aider = "aider.main:main"</code> — one console script, not a plugin host.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A["main.py"] --> B["Commands(io, coder)"]
    A --> C["Coder.create(edit_format)"]
    C --> D["coders.__all__ scan&#x3C;br/>__init__.py:18-34"]
    D --> E["EditBlockCoder&#x3C;br/>WholeFileCoder&#x3C;br/>ArchitectCoder ..."]
    B --> F["Commands.run(inp)"]
    F --> G{"starts with / or !?"}
    G -->|/cmd| H["do_run → cmd_*"]
    G -->|!| I["do_run('run', ...)"]
    H --> J["SwitchCoder exception&#x3C;br/>mode / model switch"]
    H --> K["Side effects:&#x3C;br/>web, lint, git"]
    E --> L["get_edits / apply_edits&#x3C;br/>format-specific"]
</code></pre>
<p>Runtime "plugins" are <strong>classes already imported</strong> at startup — not DLL-style modules loaded from disk.</p>
<h2><code>Commands</code> class — slash-command registry</h2>
<h3>Construction and cloning</h3>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/commands.py:36-85</code> defines <code>Commands</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">class Commands:
    voice = None
    scraper = None

    def clone(self):
        return Commands(
            self.io,
            None,
            voice_language=self.voice_language,
            ...
        )

    def __init__(self, io, coder, ...):
        self.io = io
        self.coder = coder
        ...
</code></pre>
<p>When switching coders via <code>SwitchCoder</code>, <code>Coder.create(from_coder=...)</code> copies <code>commands=from_coder.commands.clone()</code> (<code>base_coder.py:177</code>) so slash handlers persist across edit-format changes.</p>
<h3>Convention-based registration</h3>
<p>The authoritative comment at <code>commands.py:334-335</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># any method called cmd_xxx becomes a command automatically.
# each one must take an args param.
</code></pre>
<p>Discovery is reflection over <code>dir(self)</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python"># commands.py:276-285
def get_commands(self):
    commands = []
    for attr in dir(self):
        if not attr.startswith("cmd_"):
            continue
        cmd = attr[4:]
        cmd = cmd.replace("_", "-")
        commands.append("/" + cmd)
    return commands
</code></pre>
<p>Examples mapped:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Method</th>
<th>Slash command</th>
<th>Docstring summary</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>cmd_run</code></td>
<td><code>/run</code></td>
<td>Run shell, optional chat injection (<code>1013-1053</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cmd_web</code></td>
<td><code>/web</code></td>
<td>Scrape URL to markdown (<code>219-253</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cmd_architect</code></td>
<td><code>/architect</code></td>
<td>Switch to architect mode (<code>1190-1192</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cmd_lint</code></td>
<td><code>/lint</code></td>
<td>Lint and optionally fix (<code>356-409</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cmd_model</code></td>
<td><code>/model</code></td>
<td>Switch main LLM (<code>87-112</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cmd_chat_mode</code></td>
<td><code>/chat-mode</code></td>
<td>Switch edit format / mode (<code>138-207</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cmd_help</code></td>
<td><code>/help</code></td>
<td>Interactive help via HelpCoder (<code>1119-1144</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>No registration table, no JSON manifest, no priority ordering beyond <code>dir()</code> iteration (sorted only when displayed in <code>basic_help()</code> at <code>1104-1115</code>).</p>
<h3>Dispatch pipeline</h3>
<p><code>commands.py:312-332</code> — <code>run(inp)</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def run(self, inp):
    if inp.startswith("!"):
        self.coder.event("command_run")
        return self.do_run("run", inp[1:])

    res = self.matching_commands(inp)
    ...
    return self.do_run(command, rest_inp)
</code></pre>
<p><code>do_run()</code> at <code>287-298</code> resolves <code>cmd_{name}</code> via <code>getattr</code> and invokes with args string.</p>
<p>Completion hooks: optional <code>completions_{cmd}</code> and <code>completions_raw_{cmd}</code> methods (<code>266-274</code>, <code>258-264</code>).</p>
<h3><code>SwitchCoder</code> — runtime mode switch without plugins</h3>
<p>Model and mode changes raise <code>SwitchCoder</code> (<code>commands.py:30-33</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">class SwitchCoder(Exception):
    def __init__(self, placeholder=None, **kwargs):
        self.kwargs = kwargs
        self.placeholder = placeholder
</code></pre>
<p>Example — <code>/model</code> at <code>commands.py:96-112</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">model = models.Model(model_name, ...)
models.sanity_check_models(self.io, model)
raise SwitchCoder(main_model=model, edit_format=new_edit_format)
</code></pre>
<p><code>main.py</code> catches this exception and re-creates the coder via <code>Coder.create(**kwargs)</code> — a <strong>factory swap</strong>, not loading a new plugin module.</p>
<h3><code>/chat-mode</code> — enumerates coder registry</h3>
<p><code>cmd_chat_mode</code> at <code>commands.py:138-207</code> imports <code>aider.coders</code> and builds valid formats from <strong><code>coders.__all__</code></strong>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">valid_formats = OrderedDict(
    sorted(
        (
            coder.edit_format,
            coder.__doc__.strip().split("\n")[0] if coder.__doc__ else "No description",
        )
        for coder in coders.__all__
        if getattr(coder, "edit_format", None)
    )
)
</code></pre>
<p>Built-in aliases (<code>help</code>, <code>ask</code>, <code>code</code>, <code>architect</code>, <code>context</code>) map to edit formats or special coders before raising <code>SwitchCoder</code>.</p>
<p>This is the user-facing "plugin picker" — but every option is compiled into the package.</p>
<h3>Help command spawns another coder</h3>
<p><code>cmd_help</code> at <code>1137-1144</code> demonstrates nested factory use:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">coder = Coder.create(
    io=self.io,
    from_coder=self.coder,
    edit_format="help",
    summarize_from_coder=False,
    map_tokens=512,
    map_mul_no_files=1,
)
</code></pre>
<p><code>HelpCoder</code> is just another entry in <code>__all__</code> — not a downloaded plugin.</p>
<h2><code>Coder.create</code> — edit-format factory</h2>
<h3>Classmethod signature and selection loop</h3>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/coders/base_coder.py:124-201</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">@classmethod
def create(
    self,
    main_model=None,
    edit_format=None,
    io=None,
    from_coder=None,
    summarize_from_coder=True,
    **kwargs,
):
    import aider.coders as coders
    ...
    for coder in coders.__all__:
        if hasattr(coder, "edit_format") and coder.edit_format == edit_format:
            res = coder(main_model, io, **kwargs)
            res.original_kwargs = dict(kwargs)
            return res

    valid_formats = [...]
    raise UnknownEditFormat(edit_format, valid_formats)
</code></pre>
<p>Selection algorithm:</p>
<ol>
<li>Resolve <code>edit_format</code> from argument, <code>from_coder</code>, or <code>main_model.edit_format</code> (<code>142-148</code>).</li>
<li>If switching coders, merge kwargs from <code>from_coder.original_kwargs</code> and optionally summarize chat history on format change (<code>153-188</code>).</li>
<li>Linear scan <strong><code>coders.__all__</code></strong> for matching <code>edit_format</code> class attribute.</li>
<li>Instantiate matching subclass: <code>coder(main_model, io, **kwargs)</code>.</li>
<li>Store <code>original_kwargs</code> on instance for future switches.</li>
</ol>
<p><code>clone()</code> at <code>203-205</code> delegates to <code>Coder.create(from_coder=self, **kwargs)</code>.</p>
<h3>Default class attributes</h3>
<p><code>base_coder.py:117-118</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">suggest_shell_commands = True
detect_urls = True
</code></pre>
<p>Subclasses override <code>edit_format</code>, <code>gpt_prompts</code>, and behavior hooks (<code>get_edits</code>, <code>apply_edits</code>, <code>reply_completed</code>).</p>
<h3>Main entry wiring</h3>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/main.py:973-1007</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">coder = Coder.create(
    main_model=main_model,
    edit_format=args.edit_format,
    io=io,
    repo=repo,
    ...
    commands=commands,
    suggest_shell_commands=args.suggest_shell_commands,
    ...
)
</code></pre>
<p>The <code>commands</code> object is injected — typically constructed earlier in <code>main()</code> with shared <code>io</code>.</p>
<h2><code>coders/__init__.py</code> — exported coder list</h2>
<p>Full registry at <code>110_aider/aider/coders/__init__.py:1-34</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">from .architect_coder import ArchitectCoder
from .ask_coder import AskCoder
from .base_coder import Coder
from .context_coder import ContextCoder
from .editblock_coder import EditBlockCoder
from .editblock_fenced_coder import EditBlockFencedCoder
from .editor_diff_fenced_coder import EditorDiffFencedCoder
from .editor_editblock_coder import EditorEditBlockCoder
from .editor_whole_coder import EditorWholeFileCoder
from .help_coder import HelpCoder
from .patch_coder import PatchCoder
from .udiff_coder import UnifiedDiffCoder
from .udiff_simple import UnifiedDiffSimpleCoder
from .wholefile_coder import WholeFileCoder

__all__ = [
    HelpCoder,
    AskCoder,
    Coder,
    EditBlockCoder,
    EditBlockFencedCoder,
    WholeFileCoder,
    PatchCoder,
    UnifiedDiffCoder,
    UnifiedDiffSimpleCoder,
    ArchitectCoder,
    EditorEditBlockCoder,
    EditorWholeFileCoder,
    EditorDiffFencedCoder,
    ContextCoder,
]
</code></pre>
<p>Adding a new edit format requires:</p>
<ol>
<li>New module <code>foo_coder.py</code> subclassing <code>Coder</code>.</li>
<li>Set class attr <code>edit_format = "foo"</code>.</li>
<li>Import + append to <code>__all__</code>.</li>
<li>Optionally add prompts module and CLI docs.</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>No runtime discovery</strong> — missing step 3 means <code>UnknownEditFormat</code> at <code>base_coder.py:201</code>.</p>

<p>Commented-out <code>SingleWholeFileFunctionCoder</code> shows removed/experimental formats stay out of <code>__all__</code> (<code>__init__.py:16-17</code>, <code>28</code>).</p>
<h2>Architect pattern — two-stage coder factory</h2>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/coders/architect_coder.py:11-48</code> — not a plugin hook, but <strong>composition via factory</strong>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">def reply_completed(self):
    ...
    kwargs["main_model"] = editor_model
    kwargs["edit_format"] = self.main_model.editor_edit_format
    kwargs["suggest_shell_commands"] = False
    ...
    editor_coder = Coder.create(**new_kwargs)
    editor_coder.run(with_message=content, preproc=False)
</code></pre>
<p>The architect "plugin" is hard-coded: spawn editor coder from <code>__all__</code>, disable shell suggestions on editor pass (<code>architect_coder.py:27</code>).</p>
<h2>Config vs plugins</h2>
<p><code>110_aider/aider/args.py</code> (referenced from <code>commands.py:46</code>) defines CLI flags — edit format, models, lint commands, analytics. <code>.aider.conf.yml</code> merges into args at startup.</p>
<p>Config can point to <strong>external linter shell commands</strong> but does not load Python extension modules. Contrast Codex plugin manifest declaring MCP servers and hook scripts.</p>
<h2>GUI entry — parallel front-end</h2>
<p><code>aider/gui.py</code> (Streamlit) reuses <code>Coder.create</code> per website docs (<code>aider/website/docs/scripting.md:72-95</code>). Same coder registry, different IO wrapper — still no plugin.json.</p>

<h2>How to extend Aider (developer guide from corpus)</h2>
<h3>Add a slash command</h3>
<ol>
<li>Add <code>def cmd_foo(self, args):</code> with docstring to <code>commands.py</code>.</li>
<li><code>/foo</code> appears automatically via <code>get_commands()</code>.</li>
<li>Optionally add <code>completions_foo()</code> for tab completion.</li>
</ol>
<h3>Add an edit format</h3>
<ol>
<li>Create <code>aider/coders/myformat_coder.py</code>:
<ul>
<li><code>class MyFormatCoder(Coder):</code></li>
<li><code>edit_format = "myformat"</code></li>
<li>Implement <code>get_edits()</code> / <code>apply_edits()</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Register in <code>coders/__init__.py</code> imports and <code>__all__</code>.</li>
<li>Document in website edit formats page.</li>
</ol>
<h3>What you cannot do without forking</h3>
<ul>
<li>Load <code>.py</code> plugins from user config path at runtime.</li>
<li>Register MCP tools from manifest.</li>
<li>Inject hooks before/after model calls (no hook bus).</li>
<li>Ship closed-source extensions without vendoring into <code>aider</code> package.</li>
</ul>

41:T5549,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>Aider's safety model is <strong>human-in-the-loop confirmation</strong> via the IO layer. Shell runs, architect handoff, file additions, pip installs, gitignore prompts, URL ingestion, and lint/test recovery all call <code>confirm_ask</code> with varying strictness (<code>explicit_yes_required</code>, <code>allow_never</code>, <code>ConfirmGroup</code>). There is no autonomous guardian model, risk classifier, or policy DSL — only synchronous terminal or GUI prompts backed by <code>InputOutput</code> in <code>110_aider/aider/io.py</code>.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 012_guardian-approval/12_ai_guardian.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Aider Guardian / Approval</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>110_aider/</code> — interactive <code>io.confirm_ask()</code> gates; no policy engine or guardian agent.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Aider's safety model is <strong>human-in-the-loop confirmation</strong> via the IO layer. Shell runs, architect handoff, file additions, pip installs, gitignore prompts, URL ingestion, and lint/test recovery all call <code>confirm_ask</code> with varying strictness (<code>explicit_yes_required</code>, <code>allow_never</code>, <code>ConfirmGroup</code>). There is no autonomous guardian model, risk classifier, or policy DSL — only synchronous terminal or GUI prompts backed by <code>InputOutput</code> in <code>110_aider/aider/io.py</code>.</p>

<h2><code>confirm_ask</code> full API (<code>io.py:807-925</code>)</h2>
<p>Signature and decorator:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">@restore_multiline
def confirm_ask(
    self,
    question,
    default="y",
    subject=None,
    explicit_yes_required=False,
    group=None,
    allow_never=False,
) -> bool
</code></pre>
<h3>Parameters</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Param</th>
<th>Type</th>
<th>Default</th>
<th>Behavior</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>question</code></td>
<td><code>str</code></td>
<td>required</td>
<td>Prompt text; options suffix appended internally</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>default</code></td>
<td><code>str</code></td>
<td><code>"y"</code></td>
<td>Empty input / EOF → this value; drives <code>[Yes]</code> / <code>[No]</code> hint</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>subject</code></td>
<td><code>str | None</code></td>
<td><code>None</code></td>
<td>Bold context block printed before prompt; multiline subjects padded to max line width</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>explicit_yes_required</code></td>
<td><code>bool</code></td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
<td>When <code>self.yes is True</code> (<code>--yes-always</code>), still returns <strong>False</strong> unless user types <code>y</code>; <code>(A)ll</code> disabled in group mode</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>group</code></td>
<td><code>ConfirmGroup | None</code></td>
<td><code>None</code></td>
<td>Batch mode for multi-item loops; forces <code>allow_never=True</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>allow_never</code></td>
<td><code>bool</code></td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
<td>Adds <code>(D)on't ask again</code>; stores <code>(question, subject)</code> in <code>never_prompts</code> → future calls return False</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>Response options (interactive)</h3>
<p>Base: <code>(Y)es/(N)o</code>. With <code>group</code>: <code>/(A)ll</code> (unless <code>explicit_yes_required</code>) and <code>/(S)kip all</code>. With <code>allow_never</code>: <code>/(D)on't ask again</code>.</p>
<p>Valid prefixes: <code>yes</code>, <code>no</code>, <code>skip</code>, <code>all</code>, <code>don't</code> (when allowed). First character drives outcome after lowercasing.</p>
<h3>Return value</h3>
<p>Returns <code>True</code> when user affirms. Affirmation means <code>res == "y"</code>, or <code>res in ("y", "a")</code> when <code>explicit_yes_required=False</code>. <code>(A)ll</code> sets <code>group.preference = "all"</code>; <code>(S)kip all</code> sets <code>"skip"</code>. <code>(D)on't ask again</code> adds to <code>never_prompts</code> and returns False.</p>
<h3>Non-interactive bypass (<code>self.yes</code>)</h3>
<p><code>InputOutput.__init__</code> stores CLI <code>--yes-always</code> as <code>self.yes</code> (<code>io.py:308</code>). Logic at <code>866-872</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>self.yes is True</code> → auto <code>"y"</code> unless <code>explicit_yes_required</code> (then auto <code>"n"</code>)</li>
<li><code>self.yes is False</code> → auto <code>"n"</code></li>
<li><code>group.preference</code> set → reuse without re-prompting</li>
</ul>
<p>Pipe mode and GUI set this explicitly: <code>main.py:546-547</code> forces <code>yes_always=True</code> when <code>return_coder=True</code> (GUI bootstrap); <code>gui.py:77-79</code> constructs <code>CaptureIO(..., yes=True, ...)</code>.</p>
<h3>Side effects</h3>
<p>Increments <code>num_user_asks</code>, may <code>ring_bell()</code>, appends blockquoted line to chat history, uses <code>prompt_session.prompt</code> or plain <code>input</code>, validates response in a loop with <code>tool_error</code> on bad input.</p>
<h3><code>ConfirmGroup</code> (<code>io.py:82-88</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python">class ConfirmGroup:
    preference: str = None  # "all" | "skip" after first batch answer
    show_group: bool = True

    def __init__(self, items=None):
        if items is not None:
            self.show_group = len(items) > 1
</code></pre>
<p>When <code>show_group</code> is False (single item), group batch options are suppressed. Used for URL lists, file mentions, and shell command batches.</p>
<h3><code>never_prompts</code></h3>
<p>Set of <code>(question, subject)</code> tuples. Checked at start of <code>confirm_ask</code> and in <code>offer_url</code>. Persists for session lifetime only (not disk).</p>
<h3>Related: <code>offer_url</code> (<code>io.py:797-804</code>)</h3>
<p>Wraps <code>confirm_ask(prompt, subject=url, allow_never=allow_never)</code> then <code>webbrowser.open(url)</code> on True.</p>

<p>Codex routes shell/patch/network/MCP through guardian review; Aider routes the same classes of work through ~20 distinct <code>confirm_ask</code> strings with no central registry.</p>
<hr>
<h2>Interactive prompt construction (detail)</h2>
<p>When not bypassed by <code>self.yes</code>, <code>confirm_ask</code> builds the prompt string incrementally (<code>io.py:831-846</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>Start with bare <code>question</code>.</li>
<li>Append <code> (Y)es/(N)o</code>.</li>
<li>If <code>group</code> active and not <code>explicit_yes_required</code>, append <code>/(A)ll</code>.</li>
<li>If <code>group</code> active, append <code>/(S)kip all</code> (works even with <code>explicit_yes_required</code> — skip still available).</li>
<li>If <code>allow_never</code> (forced True when <code>group</code> set), append <code>/(D)on't ask again</code>.</li>
<li>Append default hint: <code>[Yes]</code>, <code>[No]</code>, or <code>[{default}]</code>.</li>
</ol>
<p>The <code>subject</code> block renders <strong>before</strong> the question line when present. Multiline subjects pad every line to the longest line width so block commands (shell batches) align in the terminal.</p>
<p>Input loop uses prefix matching: <code>any(valid_response.startswith(res) for valid_response in valid_responses)</code> so <code>y</code>, <code>ye</code>, <code>yes</code> all work. Invalid input prints <code>Please answer with one of: …</code> via <code>tool_error</code> and retries.</p>
<p>Chat history records blockquoted <code>{question_stripped} {first_char}</code> for auditability in <code>--chat-history-file</code> sessions.</p>
<hr>
<h2><code>--yes-always</code> vs <code>explicit_yes_required</code> matrix</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><code>self.yes</code></th>
<th><code>explicit_yes_required</code></th>
<th>Result without user input</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>True</code></td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
<td><strong>True</strong> (auto yes)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>True</code></td>
<td><code>True</code></td>
<td><strong>False</strong> (auto no — shell safety)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>False</code></td>
<td>any</td>
<td><strong>False</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>None</code></td>
<td>any</td>
<td>interactive prompt</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Call sites using <code>explicit_yes_required=True</code>: only <code>base_coder.handle_shell_commands</code> (<code>2456-2461</code>). Every other gate respects <code>--yes-always</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>Onboarding and OAuth (adjacent, not in scope table)</h2>
<p><code>onboarding.py:93-96</code> calls <code>confirm_ask("Login to OpenRouter or create a free account?", default="y")</code>. This is onboarding surface, not execution guardian, but uses the same API and respects <code>self.yes</code>. Documented for completeness; WP53 call-site list focuses on <code>base_coder</code>, <code>commands</code>, <code>scrape</code>, <code>main</code>, <code>utils</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>Test coverage pointers</h2>
<p><code>tests/basic/test_io.py</code> exercises <code>explicit_yes_required</code>, <code>ConfirmGroup</code> all/skip, <code>allow_never</code>, yes/no parsing. <code>tests/basic/test_coder.py</code> mocks <code>confirm_ask</code> for shell and architect flows. Tests confirm GUI/pipe behavior is simulated via <code>self.yes</code>, not separate code paths.</p>
<hr>
<h2>Boundary (explicit non-goals)</h2>
<ul>
<li>No autonomous guardian model or risk classifier</li>
<li>No policy DSL or TOML permission profiles</li>
<li>No structured approval request type or wire protocol</li>
<li>No fail-closed timeout path — missing stdin EOF uses <code>default</code></li>
<li><code>never_prompts</code> is session-scoped, not project-scoped</li>
</ul>
<p>Approval is synchronous <code>InputOutput</code> only; GUI replaces IO on <code>coder.commands.io</code> but inherits the same <code>confirm_ask</code> implementation via <code>CaptureIO(InputOutput)</code>.</p>
<hr>

42:T13bad,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>Aider는 dimensions 01-12 (TUI, Prompt, Tool, Skill, Subagent, Surface, Sandbox, Config, MCP, Memory, Plugin, Guardian)에 포함되지 않는 고유한 교차 관심사들을 다수 보유하고 있다. 특히 <strong>Git/VCS 통합</strong>과 <strong>Coder 전략 다양성</strong>은 Aider를 다른 AI 코딩 에이전트와 차별화하는 핵심 강점이다.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>개요</li>
<li>
<ol>
<li>Git/VCS 통합 (핵심 강점)</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>1.1 아키텍처 개요</li>
<li>1.2 GitRepo 클래스 (<code>repo.py</code>)</li>
<li>1.3 RepoMap - Tree-sitter + PageRank (<code>repomap.py</code>)</li>
<li>1.4 .aiderignore 시스템</li>
<li>
<ol start="2">
<li>모델 라우팅 / 프로바이더 추상화</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>2.1 아키텍처</li>

<pre><code class="language-python"># repo.py - Attribution 핵심 로직
@contextlib.contextmanager
def set_git_env(var_name, value, original_value):
    """Temporarily set a Git environment variable."""
    os.environ[var_name] = value
    try:
        yield
    finally:
        if original_value is not None:
            os.environ[var_name] = original_value
        elif var_name in os.environ:
            del os.environ[var_name]
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-python"># repo.py - get_commit_message()
def get_commit_message(self, diffs, context, user_language=None):
    diffs = "# Diffs:\n" + diffs
    content = ""
    if context:
        content += context + "\n"
    content += diffs

    system_content = self.commit_prompt or prompts.commit_system
    # 사용자 언어 설정 지원
    if user_language:
        language_instruction = f"\n- Is written in {user_language}."
    system_content = system_content.format(language_instruction=language_instruction)

    # 다중 모델 폴백: 토큰 한도 초과 시 다음 모델로
    for model in self.models:
        num_tokens = model.token_count(messages)
        max_tokens = model.info.get("max_input_tokens") or 0
        if max_tokens and num_tokens > max_tokens:
            continue
        commit_message = model.simple_send_with_retries(messages)
        if commit_message:
            break
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-python"># repomap.py - Tag = namedtuple("Tag", "rel_fname fname line name kind")
def get_tags_raw(self, fname, rel_fname):
    lang = filename_to_lang(fname)
    language = get_language(lang)
    parser = get_parser(lang)

    # Tree-sitter 쿼리 파일 (.scm) 로드
    query_scm = get_scm_fname(lang)
    code = self.io.read_text(fname)
    tree = parser.parse(bytes(code, "utf-8"))

    # 캡처 실행
    captures = self._run_captures(Query(language, query_scm), tree.root_node)

    for node, tag in all_nodes:
        if tag.startswith("name.definition."):
            kind = "def"
        elif tag.startswith("name.reference."):
            kind = "ref"
        yield Tag(rel_fname=rel_fname, fname=fname,
                  name=node.text.decode("utf-8"), kind=kind,
                  line=node.start_point[0])

    # ref가 없으면 Pygments로 백필
    if "ref" not in saw and "def" in saw:
        lexer = guess_lexer_for_filename(fname, code)
        tokens = [t[1] for t in lexer.get_tokens(code) if t[0] in Token.Name]
        for token in tokens:
            yield Tag(..., name=token, kind="ref", line=-1)
</code></pre>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-python"># repomap.py - get_ranked_tags()
def get_ranked_tags(self, chat_fnames, other_fnames, mentioned_fnames, mentioned_idents):
    import networkx as nx

    G = nx.MultiDiGraph()
    personalize = 100 / len(fnames)

    # 가중치 계산 - 다중 휴리스틱
    for ident in idents:
        mul = 1.0
        if ident in mentioned_idents:    mul *= 10    # 대화에서 언급된 식별자
        is_snake = ("_" in ident)                      # snake_case
        is_camel = any(c.isupper() for c in ident)     # camelCase
        if (is_snake or is_camel) and len(ident) >= 8:
            mul *= 10                                   # 긴 의미있는 이름
        if ident.startswith("_"):  mul *= 0.1           # 프라이빗
        if len(defines[ident]) > 5: mul *= 0.1          # 너무 많은 정의 = 일반적

        for referencer, num_refs in Counter(references[ident]).items():
            for definer in definers:
                use_mul = mul
                if referencer in chat_rel_fnames:
                    use_mul *= 50  # 대화 중인 파일에서의 참조 = 매우 중요
                num_refs = math.sqrt(num_refs)  # 빈도 스케일 다운
                G.add_edge(referencer, definer, weight=use_mul * num_refs)

    # PageRank 실행
    ranked = nx.pagerank(G, weight="weight", personalization=personalization)
</code></pre>

# 순위화된 태그를 이진 탐색으로 토큰 예산에 맞춤
middle = min(int(max_map_tokens // 25), num_tags)
while lower_bound &#x3C;= upper_bound:
    tree = self.to_tree(ranked_tags[:middle], chat_rel_fnames)
    num_tokens = self.token_count(tree)
    pct_err = abs(num_tokens - max_map_tokens) / max_map_tokens
    if pct_err &#x3C; 0.15:  # 15% 오차 허용
        break
    if num_tokens &#x3C; max_map_tokens:
        lower_bound = middle + 1
    else:
        upper_bound = middle - 1
    middle = int((lower_bound + upper_bound) // 2)

<pre><code class="language-python"># repo.py - pathspec 기반 gitignore 호환 패턴 매칭
def refresh_aider_ignore(self):
    if not self.aider_ignore_file:
        return
    # 1초 미만 간격 체크 방지 (성능)
    current_time = time.time()
    if current_time - self.aider_ignore_last_check &#x3C; 1:
        return
    # mtime 기반 변경 감지
    mtime = self.aider_ignore_file.stat().st_mtime
    if mtime != self.aider_ignore_ts:
        self.aider_ignore_ts = mtime
        self.ignore_file_cache = {}
        lines = self.aider_ignore_file.read_text().splitlines()
        self.aider_ignore_spec = pathspec.PathSpec.from_lines(
            pathspec.patterns.GitWildMatchPattern, lines)
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-python"># llm.py - litellm import가 1.5초 걸리므로 지연 로딩
class LazyLiteLLM:
    _lazy_module = None

    def __getattr__(self, name):
        if name == "_lazy_module":
            return super()
        self._load_litellm()
        return getattr(self._lazy_module, name)

    def _load_litellm(self):
        if self._lazy_module is not None:
            return
        self._lazy_module = importlib.import_module("litellm")
        self._lazy_module.suppress_debug_info = True
        self._lazy_module.set_verbose = False
        self._lazy_module.drop_params = True
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-python">def get_ex_info(self, ex):
    # boto3 미설치 시 명확한 안내
    if ex.__class__ is litellm.APIConnectionError:
        if "boto3" in str(ex):
            return ExInfo("APIConnectionError", False, "You need to: pip install boto3")
    # 크레딧 부족 시 재시도 안 함
    if ex.__class__ is litellm.APIError:
        if "insufficient credits" in str(ex).lower() and '"code":402' in str(ex).lower():
            return ExInfo("APIError", False, "Insufficient credits.")
